Hitler's Written Note Brought to Paris by the French Counselor

Troop Size Increased to 300,000, Equal Defense Weapons

Sign a Non-Aggression Treaty for a Term of Ten Years

Saar Returns to Germany, Mineral Resources Still Under French Control

(Paris) Qingyi Newspaper published a telegram from its Berlin correspondent, saying that the Chief Counselor of the French Embassy in Germany, Arna, took the German reply and set off for France at 10:00 PM last night. This reply was sent by the German government to the French Ambassador to Germany, Pongse, yesterday. The content is to explain Germany's demands for rearmament, which are generally the same as the points that we have repeatedly reported in advance, namely: (1) The number of active troops will be increased to 300,000; (2) Defense weapons should be equal to those of other European countries without restrictions; (3) Germany proposed to France to sign a non-aggression treaty for a term of ten years. (19th Day Havas Telegram)

(Paris) French Ambassador to Germany, Arna, arrived here this morning with the German reply and has presented the documents to the Confidential Secretary of Foreign Minister Peng Gu. The content is a kind of written note, but the requirements for the number of troops and weapons are not formal diplomatic documents of the German government. These documents are expected to be sent to the ambassadors of Britain and Italy at the same time. After receiving them, the French government will hold a cabinet meeting to discuss them and then send instructions to the French Ambassador to Germany, Pongse, that are in line with the situation. In addition to the items mentioned in the previous telegram, the content of the German note also recognizes that the party army of the National Socialist Party is subject to international supervision, but only if military groups other than the official armies of other countries are also subject to supervision. Regarding the Saar mining area, Germany requests that it be returned to Germany without going through a referendum, but the mineral resources and other properties there will still be controlled by France before 1935. (19th Day Havas Telegram)

(Paris) The documents that the German government sent to the French Ambassador to Germany, Pongse, regarding the armament issue were taken back yesterday by the Chief Counselor of the French Embassy, Arna. The newspapers paid great attention to this matter, saying that this document is not a diplomatic note from the German government, but only that Hitler sent his opinions to the French ambassador in writing after talking with Pongse. The Chen Bao said that the French government does not need to reply to this proposal with another note, but only needs to instruct Pongse with its opinions, which is sufficient. In addition, the newspapers all believe that the German submission will undoubtedly faithfully express the German views and are convinced that the German Ministry of Foreign Affairs will send these documents to London and Rome at the same time. The newspapers all agreed that the various demands made by Germany cannot be accepted. The Excelsior said that the German note contains the maximum demands, intending to leave room for maneuver so that Britain and Italy can mediate. The Business Daily said that the German demands are a formal attempt to rearm, while French policy advocates security first, then disarmament. In comparison, the German proposal cannot be recognized at all. All eyes are focused on the meeting between British Foreign Secretary Simon and French Foreign Minister Peng Gu at the end of this week. (20th Day Havas Telegram)

(Paris) Paris has received today the German written suggestions, this happening should facilitate the meeting between the French and British Foreign Ministers Peng Gu and Simon on Friday. Whatever beneficial results the Franco-British talk may bring, it can be clear that the French government are holding a negative feeling that Hitler's demands cannot be received, it is unlikely that Britain will recommend it be changed, is the German memorandum to hand, confirming the previous transmitted requests of the several items, inside, there is one wishing to conclude an accord for the establishment of a ten-year mutual non-aggression pact. (20th Day Reuters Telegram)

French Parliament Passes Military Preparedness Reorganization

Active Troops Number 468,000

Recruiting 15,000 Technical Specialists

Enlistment Period to Increase by Four Months

(Paris) During the European War, France's birth rate decreased. By 1936, there was a significant shortage of adults eligible for military service. To remedy this, the government drafted a bill to increase the conscription age by four months. Today, the Chamber of Deputies passed this bill with a majority of 449 votes to 147, allowing the Army, Navy, and Air Force to change the conscription age. The bill also stipulates the recruitment of 15,000 individuals with specialized skills to compensate for the shortfall in military personnel. During the discussion, former Prime Minister Tardieu stated that this bill was a temporary measure and of little practical effect. However, his statement was refuted by Mr. Foburi, the chairman of the Military Affairs Committee, and also by Minister of War Daladier, whose speech was warmly received. Tardieu briefly stated that some people believe France cannot defend itself and are spreading rumors to unsettle the public, which is a mistake. France currently has a standing army of 468,000 men. In addition, there are reservists and troops available for conscription, totaling 500,000, all of whom have received complete training. The funds approved by the Chamber are to be used to procure modern military equipment. Without this equipment, soldiers would only be sacrificed, repeating the mistakes of 1916. France's defense organization is unparalleled in the world and in history. Minister of War requested the Chamber to approve further funding so that defense facilities could be extended to the coast. Daladier does not believe that a nation can be destroyed and subjected to tyranny by an army of 500,000 men. Daladier continued, saying that the comprehensive strength of the nation's young men is the primary energy of the country. The current issue is how to arm, command, and conscript these young men under the best possible conditions. Daladier continued, "No matter how complex the situation, France must be able to observe the changes calmly and be able to cope with any unforeseen events. The bill proposed by the government is very clear." Daladier concluded, "Regarding military affairs, the Chamber has two paths: either follow the government's request and pass the bill to remedy the inadequacy of military personnel, especially to recruit model troops to strengthen border defenses; or, if not, then the term of military service will be increased to eighteen months or two years. You must choose for yourselves," and so on. After several people spoke, the Chamber finally agreed with the government's opinion (Havas dispatch on the 19th).

(Paris) Former Prime Minister Tardieu, while debating in the Chamber of Deputies today on the proposal to postpone the conscription of recruits from 1934 to 1936, stated that the spring of 1934 would be a perilous time for Europe and France. He opposed reducing the size of the army in the spring of 1934, saying that France urgently needed military strength to ensure peace. Minister of War Daladier replied that France could ensure its own safety because there were 468,000 soldiers listed on the active duty roster and 500,000 reservists who had received complete training. France also had excellent new weapons and defenses, unprecedented in French history. It is reported that France intends to postpone the conscription of recruits from 1934 to 1936, the purpose being to increase the number of recruits conscripted from 1936 to 1940, because the birth rate in France from 1915 to 1919 decreased, and it is predicted that there will not be many new recruits in the years before 1940 (Reuters dispatch on the 20th).

Kellogg Still Dreams of Peace

The Anti-War Pact Becomes Scrap Paper

Kellogg Still Dreams of Peace

Says That if War Breaks Out in the World

Hopes the United States Will Not Be Drawn Into the European Vortex

(New York) Former U.S. Secretary of State Kellogg, speaking at the centennial memorial banquet of the dynamite inventor Nobel here today, stated that he believed that no European or Asian country would initiate hostilities unless it were insane. He did not believe there was such danger. However, although Kellogg strongly advocated promoting the principle of arbitration, he also did not believe that it was currently the time for complete disarmament, saying that it should be reduced so as not to inspire ambitions to invade others. Finally, he said that in the event of war, he hoped that the United States would maintain a clear-headed attitude and not join the vortex (National Telegram on the 20th).

U.S. Navy Reorganization and Expansion Plan

The Coast Guard Directly Under the Navy

U.S. Navy Reorganization and Expansion Plan

The Coast Guard Directly Under Naval Command

Increased Appropriation to Build New Ships

(Washington) Today, Washington naval circles predict that the U.S. Navy is undergoing a reorganization and expansion plan. The visible signs are: (1) It is reported that the Coast Guard will be merged into the Navy; (2) The Marine Corps will be reorganized into a fleet combat team to be more closely governed by the fleets; (3) In June of this year, the U.S. President allocated $238,000,000 from the public works fund to build new ships, and then allocated an additional $57,744,490 for the expansion of the Navy. The news that the Coast Guard will be merged into the Navy was released today after a meeting at the White House between naval, Coast Guard, and Treasury Department officials. According to well-informed sources, this move will be in line with the government's policy of seeking to economize on administrative expenses. From the fact that the Navy was recently ordered to assist the Coast Guard in cracking down on liquor smuggling, it can be seen that the merger of the two is an important current task. It is heard that the Navy Secretary stated at the White House today that the Navy can handle most of the Coast Guard's work without losing its effectiveness. The Coast Guard was originally reorganized from the Customs Enforcement Team and the Life-Saving Team. Although it is under the command of the Navy Department, it is dispatched by the Treasury Department. In peacetime, its main duties are to suppress smuggling, protect taxes, rescue ships in distress, remove obstacles from waterways, and enforce navigation laws (National Telegram on the 19th).

Pan-American Conference Passes Resolution Not to Interfere in Other Countries' Internal Affairs

The United States, Peru, and Brazil Declare Reservations

(Montevideo) Today, the Pan-American Conference registered a resolution firmly opposing Western Hemisphere countries using interference in other countries as an instrument of government policy. The United States, Peru, and Brazil all declared reservations, but U.S. Secretary of State Hull declared that the United States was only temporarily reserving judgment, pending clarification of some of its clauses. However, it can be asserted that, while President Roosevelt is in office, countries need not worry about U.S. interference in their internal affairs. The reservations of Peru and Brazil are directed at the clause suggesting non-recognition of territories acquired by force, as they want to thoroughly research the clause to determine what impact it will have on the dispute over Leticia Port between Colombia and Peru before agreeing to it. Hull's declaration of reservation was also because he wanted to study whether this proposal contradicts laws containing the Monroe Doctrine and the Platt Amendment. However, Mexican Foreign Minister Casaurán had already publicly requested that the United States abandon the Monroe Doctrine and the Platt Amendment (National Telegram on the 19th).

South Manchuria Railway Reorganization Plan Plunges Saitō into a Dilemma

The Military and Various Ministries Hold Conflicting Views

South Manchuria Railway's Operating Surplus This Year Is 40 Million

North Manchuria Railway Network Plan Actively Underway

(Tokyo) Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai recently formally expressed his opposition to the South Manchuria Railway (SMR) reorganization plan in his capacity as administrator. Minister of War Araki expressed that it must be reorganized. Other ministers, such as Finance Minister Takahashi and Foreign Minister Hirota, echoed Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai and also expressed their opposition to the reorganization. Prime Minister Saitō is in a difficult position and feels very hesitant. He is worried that it will become a "cancer" within the cabinet and is quite anxious. Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai, also aware of the seriousness of the issue, paid a special visit to the Prime Minister at his official residence at 3:00 PM today to discuss comprehensive countermeasures and to negotiate on the colonial budget issue (China United Press dispatch on the 20th).

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Colonial Affairs is absolutely opposed to the reorganization plan created by the SMR and the Kwantung Army in the first step. In the second step, if reorganization is necessary, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs should submit its own reorganization plan, using a two-step strategy to counter it. The Ministry of Finance also holds the view of opposing fundamental reform, and it is inevitable that there will be a head-on conflict with the Army, which supports the on-site plan. Its impact is bound to affect the political situation. At this time, attention is being paid to the attitude of Minister of War Araki. Minister Araki's belief in supporting the Saitō Cabinet has changed since the Five-Minister Conference and the Internal Affairs Conference. He believes that there is no need to maintain it. Therefore, even if some revisions are made to the SMR reorganization plan, most of the original plan will inevitably be recognized, and it will move forward bravely beyond the fate of the current cabinet in order to achieve the plan (Dentsu dispatch on the 20th).

(4) Among the Duntuo lines, the northern loop line has been formally entrusted to SMR for operation by the "Manchu" government since August 31. Marquess of Salisbury Proposes House of Lords Reform Bill in England

Reduce the Number of Members and Increase the Power to Restrict the House of Commons

Prevent the Labour Party from Implementing Drastic Changes After Gaining Power

(London) The House of Lords met today, and there was a large attendance. The Marquess of Salisbury proposed a private bill to reform the House of Lords, advocating for reducing the number of members of the House of Lords and increasing the power of the House of Lords to delay legislative bills. Secretary of the Navy Hailsham replied on behalf of the government, saying that this bill should be discussed as soon as possible, but Labour Party leader Ponsonby said that this bill reduces the number of hereditary nobles and directly restricts royal prerogatives. He should first ask the British Emperor for instructions before proceeding with this bill. Liberal Party Marquess Reid also said that this bill will indeed restrict royal prerogatives. After discussion by the public, the House of Lords allowed the proposer, the Marquess of Salisbury, to explain the reasons.

Marquess Salisbury said that the House of Lords should seek methods to protect the country in order to prevent the recurrence of unfortunate events under the previous Labour government. Labour Party member Clynes once said that the next Labour government will abolish the House of Lords, so the House of Lords must take precautions against this. He only proposed changes in the organization of the House of Lords, striving for safety. Anything unnecessary will not be involved. This bill can give the House of Lords sufficient power to prevent the country from being thrown into the chaos of major reforms without having time to consider it calmly. This bill does not want to repeal the 1911 Parliament Act. This bill recognizes the constitutional principle that financial power belongs to the House of Commons and that final governance power belongs to the people, but financial bills or other legislative bills passed by the House of Commons may only be the judgment of the majority in the Congress, not the judgment of the people. It is proposed to organize a mixed committee of the two houses, with the Speaker as the chairman, to jointly determine currency cases, rather than the Speaker doing it alone. After the reorganization of the House of Lords, if an absolute majority rejects a case three times, the final decision should be made by the House of Commons established in the next session. The two houses have now established subcommittees to plan proposals that can make Britain safe from any hasty and dangerous changes. The current proposal is based on its proposals. Foreign affairs cannot be ignored. The old system is now deemed to be replaced by a dictatorship or a disruptive change. Britain must guard against the possibility of adverse changes in its own political system. The responsibility of the House of Lords is to reform its own organization to seek national security, so the House of Lords does only what is absolutely necessary. This bill proposes a large reduction in the hereditary members of the House of Lords, reducing them to 150, plus 150 non-hereditary members, plus royal relatives, religious leaders, and legal officials, for a total of about 320 people.

Labour Party Ponsonby moved to reject this bill, calling it a political deception that seeks to change the organization to benefit the party in power. He does not believe this bill can be taken seriously. This bill uses the reorganization of the House of Lords to seek to restrain future governments. He firmly believes that if this bill is passed, many industrial seats in the next election will be owned by the Socialist Party.

Liberal Party Viscount Esher said that this bill is based on an obviously wrong principle. Esher also mentioned the remarks made by Labour Party member Clynes, saying that the House of Lords does not need to worry about a gilded dictatorship, and Labour Party leaders should avoid the idea of dictatorship, because holding this idea will only destroy themselves.

Hailsham said that all cases are given a first reading, which is customary, so he advocated that this bill be established for the first reading, but this does not mean that the government or he personally supports this bill. The government has not yet considered this bill, so he cannot express the government's opinion on this plan. The House of Lords later approved the first reading of this bill by a vote of 84 to 35 (Reuters dispatch on the 19th).

A Study of Bird Migration

Germany's Cologne Region - According to the results of a study on bird migration by the Eisen Bird Observatory, it is proven that bird migration is a natural and automatic behavior. The bird observatory has been studying this interesting problem in the Rhine River region for a long time. Every winter, wild cranes form flocks and fly south to Africa. However, it was unknown whether this migration was due to instinct or led by older birds. Therefore, the observatory obtained 160 crane chicks, all taken from crane nests, transported them from East Prussia to Eisen, kept them there for 47 days, and then released them on September 12. After they flew out, most of them flew to the Ruhr area, where they rested for some time, as if preparing for a long-distance flight. Then, they flew south in groups, passing through the Rhine River region, then through southern France and into Italy. One of them was even found at an altitude of 6,500 feet in the Alps. Furthermore, according to reports from around the world on the study of bird migration, it can be said that it has been completely successful, and it proves that these chicks, after being raised for a long time, can still choose their direction and route to reach warm areas, without needing the guidance of their mothers. (National Telegram, 19th)

Japanese Troops Invading Chahar Withdraw to Jehol Territory

The Intention of the Japanese and Puppet Troops Is to Pursue Mutinous Soldiers

Chai Shan Visits He Yingqin to Explain Everything

Song Zheyuan Discusses the Incident in Eastern Chahar

Beiping Correspondence: The sudden intrusion of Japanese and puppet troops into eastern Chahar on the border of Jehol has drawn great attention from all parties. The truth has gradually become clear in recent days, and the matter has come to an end. The situation is described as follows:

A portion of the puppet troops in western Jehol suddenly mutinied due to the pressure of the Japanese army. More than 700 Japanese troops and more than 400 puppet troops of the 8th Division of the Japanese and puppet troops were ordered to pursue them, invading eastern Chahar from Dage and Datan in western Jehol. One unit reached Xifengyan outside Dushikou on the 14th. Huang Shouzhong and Zhang Junjie, two units of the cavalry detachment of our garrison troops outside Dushikou, withdrew to Longmensuo and Dushikou to await orders in order to avoid conflict because they did not understand the intentions of the Japanese. For a time, the situation in Chicheng was quite tense. Another unit reached Xinyingzi, Tianpinggou, and Weichenggou in the second district of Guyuan at 4:00 pm on the 12th. On the evening of the 13th, they clashed with Liu Zhenyu and Ma Jinliang, two units of our Guyuan garrison troops under Zhang Yunrong, at Hongshicha and Sandaochuan. Liu's unit suffered 3 deaths and 6 injuries. In order to avoid escalating the situation, Liu and Ma's units withdrew to Mingheng Beach to await orders. After discovering the attack by the Japanese and puppet troops, our soldiers at the front immediately telegraphed the province for instructions. Song Zheyuan, Chairman of Chahar Province, telegraphed his subordinates to strengthen their defenses and respond calmly. He also telegraphed Beiping for instructions.

Page 8

The Japanese and puppet troops did not advance further after reaching Xifengzhai and other places. Gradually, starting from the 15th, they successively withdrew to Dage and Fengning. In recent days, there have been no traces of Japanese and puppet troops in Xifengzhai and the Hongshicha and Weichenggou areas of the second district of Guyuan. Our army is currently advancing to take over the defense. The incident in eastern Chahar is expected to come to an end.

After receiving the alarm from eastern Chahar, the Beiping authorities, in addition to telegraphing Song Zheyuan to respond as appropriate, also negotiated with Chai Shan, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy. Chai Shan stated that the Japanese army's actions this time were due to the discovery of a large number of bandits in western Jehol, and that they were carrying out a joint suppression, and that they would not invade Chahar territory, let alone affect the existing relations between China and Japan. Once the bandits were suppressed, they would withdraw immediately. The authorities requested Chai Shan to telegraph the Japanese Kwantung Army to quickly withdraw the troops that had entered Chahar to avoid escalating the situation, and declared that this kind of action should not happen again in the future. If it was necessary to suppress bandits, they should be notified in advance to avoid misunderstandings. Chai Shan telegraphed our intentions to the Japanese Kwantung Army. Chai Shan returned to Beiping from Tianjin yesterday. At 10:00 am today (19th), Zhu Shiqin, a section chief from the Military Branch, visited Chai Shan at the Japanese Embassy. At 10:30, Chai Shan accompanied Zhu to Jurentang to meet with He Yingqin to explain the incident in eastern Chahar and to discuss the issue of receiving Shanhaiguan. He left at about 12:00 pm.

Since the occurrence of the problem in eastern Chahar, Song Zheyuan rushed back to Zhangjiakou from Zhangbei to take command. Qin Dechun was also ordered to return to Chahar from Beiping to assist in military affairs. Now that the Japanese and puppet troops have withdrawn east and order has gradually been restored in eastern Chahar, efforts are being made to deal with the aftermath. According to what Song said to reporters from Beiping and Tianjin in Zhangjiakou this morning, the Japanese and puppet troops that invaded eastern Chahar withdrew to the Dage and Fengning areas starting from the 15th, and the incident in eastern Chahar has come to an end. The Japanese and puppet troops' intrusion into the Chahar border this time was due to a mutiny by a portion of the puppet troops in Jehol, who crossed the border to pursue them, invading our army's defense area and clashing with our unit under Zhang Yunrong. Now that the Japanese and puppet troops have withdrawn, the Guyuan area has been extremely peaceful. Most of the bandits in Chahar Province have been suppressed, and the miscellaneous troops are being reorganized. Tang Yulin's unit has been reorganized to approximately 8,000 men. A portion of the unarmed soldiers have been transferred to Zhangjiakou for training. Tang himself is now in Zhangjiakou, expressing his willingness to hand over his troops to Chahar Province for control. Prince De of Inner Mongolia sent a letter to me on the 18th, requesting me to forward a request to the Central Government to quickly find a way to realize Inner Mongolian autonomy, etc. (December 19th)

Xingbu Recovers Guangze

The Northern Route Bandit Suppression Army Advances to the Fujian Border

Military Organ Announces Fujian Intelligence

Nanchang Correspondence: Since the Northern Route Army recovered Zixi and occupied Deshengguan, the situation on the border of Jiangxi and Fujian has changed. Previously, after the Fujian Incident occurred, Zhu, Mao, Peng, Lin, Fang, Shao, and other bandit gangs, since they did not need to take care of the southeast, used the false 3rd, 5th, and 7th Army Corps to try to break through the Central Army's central route towards Zixi and Lichuan. They also used the false 1st Army Corps and various independent divisions to detour around the right flank of the Central Army, and used the Northeast Jiangxi false 10th Army and the Yi-Gui independent divisions to try to cut off the Jiangxi-Zhejiang Road to respond to the Fujian side. However, from the 11th to the 14th, Lichuan, Yihuang, Zixi, and Guixi, among other places, were broken by the National Army's bandit suppression lines. The 58th and other columns, after clearing out the bandits in Lichuan and Zixi, took advantage of the victory and advanced eastward, crossing into Fujian to encircle and suppress them, hoping to sweep them away in one fell swoop. A telephone call from Fuzhou relayed information from the front lines that the Northern Route Army's troops under Xing Zhennan, Yao Chun, and Wu Qiwai, which were advancing towards Fujian, pursued the bandits to the vicinity of Guangze on the dawn of the 18th, and launched a fierce attack, killing many bandits and seizing more than 100 rifles. The remnants of the bandits fled in disarray towards TaiNing, JianNing, and Yanping, and joined up with the false 1st, 3rd, 5th, and 7th Army Corps. Xing's division recovered the county town of Guangze at noon on the 18th and immediately dealt with the aftermath. Since Guangze is connected to Chong'an and Shaowu, it can now be connected to Liu Heding and other troops in northern Fujian after being recovered by the Northern Route Army, forming a unified force with the Central Army on the border of Zhejiang and Fujian. From here, going east, one can directly approach Fujian.

Furthermore, according to intelligence released by the Supreme Military Organ, "Deng Shizeng is in charge of the rebel's military affairs in northern Fujian. If necessary, Jiang and Cai will personally go to command. Chen and Li are carrying out a joint operation with the Red Bandits, with the Fujian Military Commission appointing Zhu De as the commander of the false 2nd Front Army and Cai as the commander of the 1st Front Army. Their troops are indeed moving towards the Gan-Zhe border in northern Fujian. The offices of the Lu Division and Zhou Brigade in northern Fujian in Fuzhou have been automatically withdrawn, which shows their support for the Central Government. The Fujian side is extremely panicked about air defense because its air force has no combat capability. Its air defense positions are Mawuichuanshi in the east, Yanping in the west, Putianquanzhou in the south, and Showningfuan in the north. Consuls from various countries are meeting in Xiamen from time to time, and a certain country is very eager to take over Fujian, using traitors to carry out activities in Fujian, but Chen and Li are completely unaware of it," etc. (December 19th)

Sichuan Army Telegram Reports Recovery of Suiding and Xuanhan

Bandit hordes split into two routes retreating towards Tongjiang

Yang Hucheng dispatched troops from southern Shaanxi to intercept

Deng Mingjie discusses crucial points for suppressing bandits

Hankou correspondence: The Sichuan Fifth Route Army recently crossed the Qu River, with Fan Shaozeng's division on the left attacking Suiding, and Zhang Huafeng, Li Guiru, and Xu Yaoqing's three brigades on the right attacking Xuanhan. Overall commander Wang Lingji was in the center, coordinating both sides. The bandits in Suiding and Xuanhan, recognizing the official army's fierce momentum, attempted to divert attention by attacking Sanhui with their main force. Meanwhile, they constructed strong fortifications at strategic passes such as Jiangkou, Fenghuang Mountain, Tazi Mountain, Chaqi Mountain, Ezi Han, Mazongtan, Zhangjiayan, Shiguyan, and Wenjialiang to disperse the official soldiers' attacking strength. On the 16th, the Fifth Route Army launched its third general offensive, successfully recovering Jiangkou, allowing rear units to completely cross the river. At dawn on the 17th, the entire bandit Ninth Army was ordered to counterattack, engaging in a desperate battle with Yang, Li, Liu, You, and Zhu's regiments on the right flank. Ultimately, due to the increasing number of official soldiers and the failure of the bandits attacking Sanhui, they collapsed and retreated upon hearing the news. Li's regiment then occupied Ezi Han, and Zhu's regiment occupied Mazongtan, gathering at the foot of Chaqi Mountain with Yang, Liu, and You's regiments. Simultaneously, Xu's brigade crossed the river from Luoweizi, linking up with Yang's regiment. Zhang's brigade occupied the Zhangjiayan and Shiguyan line, advancing towards Xuanhan City. According to reports, Xu Yaoqing's brigade was the first to recover the city that evening. The next morning, Li Guiru's brigade also recovered Chaqi Mountain. On the left flank, Fan's division had long attacked Fenghuang Mountain near Suicheng without success, so Zhang Huafeng's brigade joined the siege. Fan's troops detoured through Wenjialiang, directly crossing into Suicheng, which was also reported to be occupied on the 18th. Wang Lingji, the overall commander of the Fifth Route Army, telegraphed Hankou on the 18th to report the victory. The original telegram read as follows: "(1) Li Guiru's brigade, and Yang Qin'an and Zhang Jinghan's regiments, recovered Chaqi Mountain at dawn on the auspicious day. The bandits split into two routes retreating towards Tongjiang, with Xu's brigade pursuing. The Fifth Route Army had already recovered Xuanhan City by evening. (2) The air squadron bombed the bandits' retreat route, demonstrating its power. (3) Zhang Huafeng supervised his troops on Tazi Mountain near Suicheng, fiercely attacking Fenghuang Mountain. The bandits are resisting stubbornly, and fierce fighting is still ongoing. (4) Fan Shaozeng's division has already occupied Suiding City. (5) Xu Yaoqing's brigade recovered Xuanhan by night, and the bandits fled towards Tongjiang. Wang Lingji sealed at midday on the auspicious day." It is reported that Wang is now at Sandengpo in Kaijiang and is about to move the general headquarters forward to join the First, Second, Third, and Fourth Routes for a major offensive against the bandits. On the Shaanxi side, Yang Hucheng has also dispatched troops to make strict deployments. If the bandits flee to Shaanxi, they will be intercepted head-on from Hanzhong. (18th)

According to Deng Mingjie, the Shanghai representative of the Sichuan Bandit Suppression Commander-in-Chief, regarding the suppression of the Red Army in Sichuan, he stated, "I recently received a telegram from Chief of Staff Deng in Chongqing confirming the 21st Army's capture of Suiding and Xuanhan. This is a major key to suppressing the Red Army in Sichuan. In other words, it is a crucial battle for pacifying the Sichuan bandits. Because of the terrain, Suixuan is very important. The bandit army must occupy Suixuan if it wants to develop towards eastern Sichuan. If we do not recapture Xuan Sui, we will have no way to attack the three counties of Tongnanba, where the bandits rely on as their base. Otherwise, not only will we not be able to eliminate the bandit atmosphere, but it may also spread. Therefore, the Red bandits concentrated their main force in these two places and launched a fierce counterattack. The 21st Army began its offensive at the beginning of the month, fighting day and night, and finally captured the two places after nearly twenty days. From the results of this battle, we can see that the main force of the bandits has been defeated. After this, we can take advantage of the situation and attack step by step. The military situation is becoming more and more optimistic. The elimination of the bandit atmosphere in northern Sichuan will not be far away," and so on. Deng also showed the telegram from Chief of Staff Guo of the Chongqing Military Headquarters as follows: (1) Fan Shaozeng's Fifth Route Army attacked Suiding City with an independent brigade in the early morning of the sixteenth (auspicious), and launched a strong attack from Laoguanmiao with the Eleventh Brigade, engaging in fierce fighting for six hours. It was not until midday that they crossed the river and occupied the Chongshi Village area on the opposite bank. The bandits then retreated to the Wanghuangguan area and fortified the highlands. In this battle, over 6,000 bandits were killed. At the same time, Wang Fangzhou's troops attacked, and artillery and aircraft bombed the bandit fortifications along the river. After six hours of night fighting, Yang and Liu's regiments crossed the river, followed by Li and You's regiments. By this time, only one or two markets in Yingshan County had not been recovered, and only three or four markets in Qu County had not been recovered. There were no traces of bandits in the major and minor Pengshan mountains. Over 2,000 members of the civilian volunteer army burned down the bandit Changsheng puppet county government. (2) The bandits, considering Suiding to be in danger, launched four attacks on the left flank of Fan Shaozeng's division in the evening of the sixteenth (auspicious), failing to succeed. In the morning of the seventeenth (evening), our Twelfth Brigade launched an offensive and occupied the highlands in the Lanzhaizi area. On the morning of the eighteenth (auspicious), continuous attacks were launched on the various units on the right flank, who also crossed the river and pounced on the bandits. Although the bandits resisted stubbornly, they could not hold on. At midday (auspicious), the bandits withdrew from Suicheng, setting fires everywhere. Fan Nanxuan's brigade and Zhou's regiment pursued into the city without stopping, and the entire brigade continued to attack the Fenghuang Mountain and Baiyan area. Division Commander Fan Shaozeng personally led the special service battalion to extinguish the remaining fires in Suicheng and eliminate lurking bandits. (3) After Wang's troops Yang, Liu, and You crossed the river, in the morning (evening), the bandit's Ninth, Twentieth, and Thirtieth Armies launched a counterattack under the cover of fog. Lin Brigade and Li Regiment engaged in hand-to-hand combat. By night, the various units had advanced to Chaqi Mountain. Xu and Zhang's two brigades also crossed the river. The bandits retreated under the cover of night. Our Xu Brigade and official regiment advanced from the right flank and occupied Xuanqian City. In this battle, the official soldiers suffered about fifteen hundred casualties, and one regimental commander and two battalion commanders were injured. The bandits suffered heavy casualties, with corpses strewn all over the fields, and twice as many casualties. The various units continued to attack fiercely. According to captured bandits, Xu Xiangqian's entire army and main cadre troops are located between Xuan and Sui, with Xianglu Mountain in Shuanghechang. Aircraft reconnaissance reveals that the bandit fortifications in Xinchang Wangjiachang Shuanghechang are very large, and there are many bandits guarding them. The Fifth Route Army continues to attack." (Guowen News Agency)

Yu Feng Cotton Mill's Petition to Chairman Chiang

Concerning Workers Forcibly Taking Cotton Yarn

Submitting this petition in reply to a previous matter: This merchant factory previously submitted a document reporting the mediation process of a labor-management dispute and the workers' forcible seizure of cotton yarn, which hindered the bank's creditor rights, requesting maintenance. On the 18th of this month, we received document No. 676 from the Wuchang headquarters, stating, "Received and noted. This case, according to the telegram from Ruan Fancai, Administrative Inspector of the First District of Henan, states, 'Regarding the labor-management dispute at the Yu Feng Cotton Mill, since the factory manager Zhao Guifen returned to Zheng in the middle of last month, mediation has continued and the conditions of both parties are not far apart. However, according to the contract, the factory should pay the workers' living expenses during the shutdown period, which are more than two months in arrears. The workers' livelihoods are difficult, and after negotiations with the factory's Zhao Guifen, the workers have obtained his consent to extract 369 pieces of cotton yarn from the factory's inventory on a micro day to temporarily maintain the workers' lives. Mediation is still ongoing. In addition to reporting to the provincial government at any time, this is hereby telegraphed.' The facts in the telegram and the petition are inconsistent. In addition to ordering the Henan Provincial Government to investigate the facts and report them for further review, you should be informed of this order." Having received this order, we found that on the 5th of this month, the factory's labor union forcibly took 369 pieces of cotton yarn in the presence of government representatives. This cotton yarn is collateral handed over to the bank by the factory, and the mortgage right belongs to the bank, not the factory's own goods. Even the factory itself has no right to dispose of it. As for Zhao Guifen's trip to Zheng last month, it was on behalf of the factory's creditor, the American merchant Shenchang Foreign Firm, as the translator for the firm's representative stationed in the factory, Stinpe. It is obvious that he had no right to agree without authorization and was forced to sign. After this incident occurred, the Shanghai Banking Association telegraphed your seat, the Central Party Department, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, the National Economic Commission, the Cotton Industry Control Committee, Chairman Liu of the Henan Provincial Government, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce on the 6th of this month, appealing for maintenance. The original telegram stated, "We have received a letter from our members, the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and the Xingye Bank, stating that the Zhengzhou Yu Feng Cotton Mill owes our three banks a large amount of debt, and the pledged cotton yarn is stored in the Yu Feng warehouse. The factory was previously shut down due to losses and has not been resolved for a long time. Now, we have received a telegram from our Zhengzhou branch stating that the labor union and the mediation committee have forcibly taken 369 pieces of pledged cotton yarn, intending to sell them to pay the workers' living expenses. The creditor rights of our banks are not guaranteed. Please find a way to stop this. The Yu Feng labor-management dispute has its own solution. The labor union's forcible extraction of the bank's collateral and the local authorities' failure to stop it will not only make it impossible for the banks in the area to operate, but also at a time when the government and the provincial authorities are working hard to promote construction and develop industry, how can we encourage the banks to do their best to assist? If our government does not quickly stop this illegal act, the banks will lose their guarantee and will have to stop all industrial loans, which will have an impact on the country's industrial future. Therefore, we appeal to you to order the Zhengzhou local authorities to quickly stop this and return the cotton yarn extracted by the labor union in full, which is what we hope for. Respectfully awaiting orders." The National Economic Commission, the Cotton Industry Control Committee, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Cotton Mill Federation, and others also telegraphed the party and government agencies separately, requesting maintenance. On the 12th of this month, the National Economic Commission, the Cotton Industry Control Committee, and the Chinese Cotton Mill Federation all received a letter from the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee stating, "According to the telegram, the bad workers of the Zhengzhou Yu Feng Cotton Mill are taking advantage of the name of the whole and destroying the factory's building doors and locks, and taking out 369 pieces of cotton yarn without authorization. Please order the cotton yarn that has been taken out to be returned in full as soon as possible to protect the factory," and so on. We are submitting this document in response. We hope that you will examine it carefully. Respectfully submitted to Chairman Chiang.

Songjiang

Brother-Killing Case Sentenced to Death

Xi Weiquan and his wife, the owners of the Yongda Rice Shop on Huayang Bridge, were shot and killed this summer. After the case was investigated and Xu Guanxiang was arrested, he confessed that the deceased's younger brother, Wei Sheng, sought revenge for losing a lawsuit over property disputes with his brother. He conspired with his concubine, Song Xiaomei, at the Jiuhua Hotel in Shanghai, and with Jiang Ahe, who is on the run, to murder his brother, promising a heavy reward after the deed was done. With this clue, the suspects Xi Weisheng and Song Xiaomei were arrested, and the main culprit Shen Ahe, as well as suspects Wu Zixiang and Shen Bingsheng, were also apprehended. After the prosecutor's interrogation, they were indicted and tried several times. The final arguments were concluded on the 18th, and today (20th) at 1:00 PM was the scheduled time for sentencing. Judge Zhang signed the order to bring the defendants to the stand and announced that the defendants Xi Weisheng, Song Xiaomei, and Shen Ahe were found guilty of murder and sentenced to death. The two defendants, Wu Zixiang and Shen Bingsheng, were sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment each. Xu Guanxiang was found not guilty.

The First Battalion of the Second Security Regiment Transferred

Bai Jizhi, the battalion commander of the First Battalion of the Second Security Regiment of Jiangsu Province, was ordered to lead his troops back to this county in the fall and defend the key passes. The day before yesterday, they suddenly received an order from the Provincial Security Department to transfer to Nantong for garrison duty. After the news spread, various local organizations telegraphed the province to request that they be retained to maintain winter security. It is unknown whether this will be approved.

Suzhou

Second Phase of Land Value Tax Collection Begins

The county's autumn survey has been approved by the Department of Finance, with an exemption of 80% and a collection rate of 92%. The county government yesterday scheduled today (21st) to begin collecting the second phase of land value tax, simultaneously setting up collection points in the old Wuxian County Office and on the east and west sides of Dongting Mountain. It also announced to all grain households to voluntarily pay into the collection points within three months after the start of collection, with penalties for late payments.

Increased Business Tax for All Industries

The County Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly received letters from the Business Tax Bureau urging them to increase the business tax quota for all industries and to fill out and submit application forms. Chairman Shi Junqing invited representatives from various industries to discuss measures yesterday afternoon (20th). However, various industries found it difficult to accept an additional layer of taxation due to the recent decline in commerce. Chairman Shi strongly persuaded them to make a reluctant increase.

Wuxi

District Chief's Scandal Exposed

Yu Yingsen, the district chief of the 12th District, submitted a report to the county government the day before yesterday, stating that Yuan Yuxiang, a former assistant in the 3rd District of this county, had a bad reputation during his tenure. After leaving office, he became a vagrant and colluded with his mistress, Hua Wenying, to implement fraudulent schemes. He had previously used Hua Wenying's beauty as bait to defraud Bao Songfu, the current district chief of the 16th District, of 70 yuan. Recently, because the 15th was the deadline for receiving funds for the district (Yu referred to himself), and the 16th was the date of the district chief's meeting, he came to the city and stayed at the First Hotel on the road. Unexpectedly, Yuan and Hua also stayed there. On the evening of the 16th, Yuan Yuxiang suddenly ordered the tea room boy, Song Min, to talk to him in his room. When he arrived in the room, Yuan Yuxiang was gone, and only his mistress, Hua Wenying, was inside, falsely accusing him of having an ambiguous affair and demanding a loan of 500 yuan. Min, considering it to be extortion, immediately left. Afterwards, Yuan gathered several unknown people, who came to coerce and intimidate him, demanding at least 50 yuan to settle the matter. This was clearly a fraudulent scheme, and he requested arrest and punishment. After receiving the report, Magistrate Yan immediately sent police to summon Yuan Yuxiang, Hua Wenying, and Yu Yingsen to the case. He opened a court with Yao Fusheng, the director of the interrogation division, to investigate. Yuan and Hua both claimed that District Chief Yu had an affair with Wenying on October 24th. Afterwards, Yu asked Shen Jizhi, the director of the public sports field, to mediate, saying that it was okay for him to pay 50 yuan. When questioned about this, Yu Yingsen confessed that they had been playing a trick. After questioning Shen Jizhi and Chen Mengqi, they all testified that District Chief Yu did offer to pay 50 yuan for a settlement. Magistrate Yan, after verifying the confession, believed that Yuan and Hua's actions were indeed improper, and that Yu Yingsen, as district chief, stayed in the city, neglecting his duties. Moreover, since he had offered 50 yuan for a settlement, it was clear that he was not completely unrelated to Hua. It was also illegal for him to present a false report to the government with accusations of a fraudulent scheme. Therefore, he ordered Yu Yingsen to be dismissed from his post and transferred to the county court for interrogation by Prosecutor Shen. After five hours, the result was an order for Yuan Yuxiang and Hua Wenying to be detained, and Yu Yingsen and the witnesses were ordered to return.

Nanhui

Labor-Management Dispute Leads to Tragedy

Recently, the Hu Shunxing sock factory in Si Dunyingfang, Fourth District, was in arrears with wages. The workers' demand for payment was unsuccessful, leading to a shutdown. Yesterday was the date the factory agreed to pay the wages. Many female workers went to the factory gate to wait for payment. Unexpectedly, Hu Qinlai, the factory owner, suddenly refused to pay and, seeing the increasing number of female workers gathering, he closed the factory gate and hired people to pour water on the open space in front of the factory, making it impossible to stand. The female workers protested loudly, and Hu Qinlai led his family and hired ruffians to beat the women severely. As a result, many female workers, including Yang Xiuying, Xi Cuilin, Shen Xiaomei, Xi Cuishi, Ni Lianying, Liu Xiuying, Wang Xiaomei, and Zhu Fengxian, were injured. In addition, the pregnant woman, Qu Wangshi, who was due to give birth soon, was fatally injured and died shortly after. Qu Xishi was also seriously injured and unable to walk. All have been taken to the county government for an inquest.

Zhenjiang

Bandits Rob Graveyard Sweepers

Jiang Shoulun, a businessman from Zhenjiang who lives in Shanghai, came to Zhenjiang with four members of his family the other day. At around 12:00 PM, they took a car from the Jiangbian Automobile Company to the family graveyard in Xiaxindian to sweep the graves. However, when the car reached the vicinity of Qiaojiamen, three bandits wearing gray uniforms and carrying long guns stopped the car. The driver knew they had encountered violence and had no choice but to stop the car. The three bandits boarded the car and searched at will, robbing the Jiang family of five gold rings and more than 20 yuan in cash. Afterwards, the three bandits left. The car continued to take the passengers to Xiaxindian and returned to Zhenjiang at around 3:00 PM, reporting the incident to the Provincial Security Department and requesting the pursuit of the bandits.

Yu Ji Wheel is Likely Lost

No Response from Shanghai to Telegrams

Jiang Yuan's Passengers Have Not Yet Arrived

丨Dispatching Three Jiang to Transport Food Today丨

The Yu Ji wheel of the Yu Da Company ran aground in the waters off Wenzhou, and the hull was severely damaged. Yesterday, it was reported that a major danger had occurred, with the hull tilting and threatening to sink. The company sent a telegram, but there was no reply. Today, it was decided to send a ship to observe. The follow-up news is divided into the following sections:

Hull in Danger

On the night of the 18th, the hull of the Yu Ji wheel tilted to one side due to the flooding of the first two compartments, uneven weight distribution, and wind and waves. Fortunately, the passengers were transferred to a nearby navy ship that night. On the 19th, the Shanghai company sent several telegrams to inquire, but according to the responsible personnel of the company, there was no reply. The company was quite anxious. Yesterday afternoon, news reached this port that the Yu Ji wheel was unable to withstand the impact of the wind and waves and was about to sink. The hull had been severely damaged and was flooded on the morning of the 19th, with no hope of salvage. It is feared that it has already sunk today.

Calls Not Going Through

Yesterday, Yu Da Company and Lianbao Insurance Company wanted to understand the extent of the damage to the ship and discuss salvage methods. In the morning, they first sent a telegram to the ship, but there was no reply. In the afternoon, they used wireless radio to call. According to people in the company, they called several times but could not reach the ship. Moreover, the outgoing calls were not accepted, indicating that the ship's electricity was not working and it was unable to send or receive telegrams. The danger to the ship is obvious.

Jiang Yuan Has Not Arrived

The Jiang Yuan warship rescued more than 100 passengers and sent them to Shanghai. The first telegram stated that they could arrive in Shanghai on the night of the 19th, or at the latest on the morning of the 20th. After all, Shanghai is only a 30-hour sea journey from Sholond Island, where the accident occurred. If a warship is traveling, it can be faster. Now it is overdue and has not arrived. When asked about the company, they also said they did not know and had no definite news. It may have been delayed due to the danger to the Yu Ji.

Passengers Fleeing

The passengers on this trip of Yu Ji who came to Shanghai were all fleeing from the war in Fuzhou. Therefore, among the one hundred and dozens of people, there were many who carried a lot of luggage, and many were families traveling together, with many women, children, elderly, and weak. Now, unfortunately, they encountered danger on the ship. They suffered material losses and mental pain as a result of avoiding the war. It is a great misfortune.

Cargo Losses

The hull is covered by a large amount of marine insurance, so Yu Da Company may not suffer significant losses. The cargo inside the ship included 4,000 buckets of oranges and more than 6,000 buckets of olives. Although the Hakka insurance company is said to have only insured 60,000 yuan, accounting for half of the cargo value, olives soaked in seawater will change color and swell, making them unsalable. Therefore, the fruit merchants and insurance companies suffered the greatest losses.

Land Value Tax Collection Begins in Shanghai's West and Zhabei Districts Today

Huazhong and Other Districts Must Wait for Continued Assessment

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the land value taxes in the southern Shanghai and Zhabei areas of the city have been assessed by the valuation committee and are scheduled to begin collection today. The remaining Huazhong and other districts will continue to be assessed. The details are as follows:

Collection Begins Today

The provisional land value tax in districts one through eight in southern Shanghai and districts one and two in Zhabei has been assessed by the valuation committee hired by the Finance and Land Bureaus. The highest land value in the city is 21,000 yuan, and the lowest is 800 yuan. The Finance Bureau has decided to start collecting taxes today. The valuation committee is still continuing to assess land values in the other areas, including Huazhong, Yinxin Special District, Pu Song, Zhenru, Wusong, Longhua, Yangsi, Yangjing, Caojing, Yinhang, Luhang, Gaohang, and Jiangwan.

Collection Method

The collection procedures will be handled by the North Shanghai Tax Collection Office of the Finance Bureau for the Zhabei area, and by the South Shanghai Tax Collection Office for the southern Shanghai area. All landowners within the collection area must, within two months from the start of collection, hold their land ownership certificate and pay the tax to the collection office in accordance with the regulations. Those who have not completed the land survey and clearance and have not exchanged for new certificates will not be accepted. The tax rate is 0.6% of the assessed land value, payable in two installments, upper and lower halves of the year. Each installment is 0.3%. If the land value is under appeal, the tax will be collected according to the assessed value determined by the public valuation. If the public ruling decides that the amount is insufficient, the deficiency must be paid up; if there is a surplus, it will be used for the next installment.

Joint Announcement

In addition to the joint announcement by the Finance and Land Bureaus regarding the collection of the provisional land value tax, a tax notice will be sent to taxpayers, detailing the location of the taxpayer's land, land area, assessed land value per mu, the amount of tax payable for this installment, the tax deadline, the tax collection agency, address, and the penalties for overdue taxes. The notice was sent out last week. If taxpayers have not received the notice due to an unknown address or relocation, they must immediately report it to the tax collection agency.

Handling Overdue Taxes

If the tax is not paid within two months from the start of collection, it will be considered overdue and will be pursued. In addition to the amount owed, an additional 5% annual interest will be levied from the day after the tax deadline. If the tax is not paid for three years, the collection agency may, with the approval of the municipal government, auction the land and any fixed assets on it to offset the overdue tax, and the surplus will be returned to the original tax debtor.

Dispatching Ship to Transport Food

Yesterday, Yu Da Company and Lianbao Company agreed that there were still some aspects of the Yu Ji's situation that were not yet clear, and decided to send a ship to investigate. After discussions with Yu Da, they consulted with Daxing Company and chartered the Three Jiang ship to set sail from Shanghai to Wenzhou Ocean this afternoon to inspect the current situation of Yu Ji and whether it can be salvaged. The company has allocated food for the crew on board, which will be delivered by Mr. Xu, the owner of the Three Jiang ship, to provide assistance. According to people in the company, in the event that the crew cannot stay on the Yu Ji ship, the navy ship Chu Guan is nearby and they can move to the ship. There is little hope for the rescue of Yu Ji. Also, Wanglai Company in this port has insured the cargo for several tens of thousands of yuan and has decided to wait until the Three Jiang ship arrives at the site to inspect before jointly discussing salvage methods.

New Culture Bookstore's Defense Letter and the Chamber of Commerce's Stern Rebuttal

Confirmed by Both Public Associations

Sufficient to Show Utmost Impartiality

Since the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce published information about the New Culture Bookstore purchasing inferior paper and printing/selling books like "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio," it has greatly attracted social attention. Yesterday, the Chamber received a defense letter from the bookstore and issued a stern rebuttal.

The direct reply stated: On the 19th of this month, we received your letter requesting the paper industry association to provide substantial evidence regarding the purchase of over ten thousand reams of paper. We are fully aware.

The fact that your bookstore uses Japanese paper was already proven by the paper industry association through the "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio" sold by your bookstore. Although the accusation was initiated by the paper industry association, the assessment was actually conducted by the book industry association. The book industry association's primary duty is to protect the interests of its members. Since the association has confirmed that it is indeed Japanese paper, it sufficiently demonstrates their utmost impartiality.

Regarding the bookstore's inspection of the paper industry, it is claimed to be "a father defending his son," which is an inappropriate statement. As for the book industry's assessment, it is dismissed as "jealousy among peers." Thus, the reports from both associations are considered untrustworthy. While the bookstore may protect itself, the Chamber cannot share the same view.

It is important to understand that the term "jealousy among peers" is applicable between bookstores. However, the position of a public association transcends individual interests, encompassing all members from A to Z. The association maintains a detached and objective stance. Therefore, the Chamber believes that the book industry association's assessment cannot be overturned by the bookstore.

Respectfully submitted to the New Culture Bookstore.

The Navy's Jungan Transport Ship Purchased by Sanbei as a Merchant Vessel

The Price is Over 300,000

In recent years, the Navy has built new ships and has leased or sold its older transport ships to various shipping companies for use as merchant vessels. In the spring of this year, the Puan, the Navy's largest tonnage ship, was leased to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and converted into a cruise ship. Now, the Jungan ship has also been priced at over 300,000 and sold to the Sanbei Shipping Company.

The Public Concession's Telephone Price Increase Plan Temporarily Withdrawn

The Telephone Company's Existing USD Debt

Will be Converted into a Silver Loan with the Assistance of the Municipal Council

At the Municipal Council meeting on the 13th of this month, the Chief Financial Officer reported that the telephone company's request for an immediate price increase was mainly due to the fact that a large portion of its investment was raised in US dollars, and the exchange rate calculated according to the agreement was attributed to the company. Therefore, the company planned to increase prices by 41% in 1935 to maintain operations.

After discussions between the Chief Financial Officer and the company, the company was advised to convert its capital entirely into silver to avoid exchange rate risks for the benefit of users. However, the company had also considered raising silver loans to repay its USD debt, but had not been able to do so. Therefore, the Chief Financial Officer suggested that the Municipal Council assist the company in completing this task, subject to the following conditions: (1) the application for an immediate price increase must be withdrawn; (2) the price increase in 1935 must not exceed 25%; (3) there must be no further price increases in the two-year period from 1935 to April 1937.

The required silver loan is approximately 6 million taels. Since the Chief Financial Officer has funds available for investment at the end of this year, it is proposed to lend 4 million taels to the company at an interest rate of 6.25%. The remaining amount can be raised locally. The Council's loan will be for a term ending at the end of 1937, but the Council can recall 500,000 to 1 million taels at any time with six months' notice, starting in 1934. This method complies with the Council's regulations and is very beneficial for general users. The public can be assured that the price increase in 1935 will be at most one-quarter, and in fact, it may not be that much.

After discussions, the Council has decided to proceed as proposed by the Chief Financial Officer. The company is currently developing a plan on how to ensure that large and small users share the price increase equally. This issue will be further studied in the future.

The Bankers Association Sent a Letter to Members Yesterday, Setting a Deadline to Report Silver Bullion Amounts

The Total Silver Bullion in the City is Approximately 130 Million Taels

A Shanghai Times reporter reports from this city that the Ministry of Finance is actively promoting the abolition of the tael and the adoption of the yuan in order to unify the currency system. Recently, the Ministry has ordered the Central Bank to send a letter to the banking industry, setting a deadline of one month for reporting all silver taels stored in the city to the Ministry of Finance. The Central Bank is authorized to exchange silver taels for silver dollars at a prescribed conversion rate (7.15). If the Central Mint's minting capacity is insufficient for full exchange, the exchange may be done on a monthly basis.

The amount of silver bullion currently stored in this city is a matter of concern to all sectors. The Shanghai Times reporter made inquiries from various sources and learned that the Bankers Association has, in accordance with the Ministry of Finance's deadline, forwarded a detailed report to its members. The Bankers Association's original letter and the survey of stored silver are recorded separately below.

Letter from the Bankers Association

Yesterday, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the Bankers Association, sent a letter to more than 30 member banks, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Central Trust of China, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and Ningbo Commercial Bank. The letter stated:

"Gentlemen, in accordance with the Central Bank's letter and the Ministry of Finance's repeated urging, for the sake of completing the abolition of the tael, this bank is specially ordered to forward to Chinese and foreign banking institutions a request to report the amount of silver bullion previously circulated on the market that is currently stored. This report must be submitted to this bank within one month for compilation and transmission to the Ministry of Finance for registration. After verification by officials dispatched by the Ministry, the banks will be allowed to exchange the silver bullion for silver coins at a rate of 7.15 per month. We should comply accordingly. In addition to sending separate letters, we are enclosing a copy of the Ministry of Finance's letter for your reference. Please forward it to your member banks for compliance and promptly respond within one month with the amount of silver bullion stored in your banks for compilation and transmission to the Ministry of Finance. We hope for your cooperation. Chairman Lin Kanghou."

Investigation of Stored Silver Bullion

Silver bullion was a silver ingot of unequal size during the old days. Their quality also varied. Without a professional appraisal, it was difficult to distinguish between good and bad. Since the import of Mexican silver into the interior, society found it convenient, and China also minted a lot. In fact, silver bullion had stopped circulating. However, the banking industry still widely used it as reserves.

This has become a habit and is difficult to abolish immediately. Bills and notes are all denominated in silver taels. Therefore, society had two units: silver taels and silver dollars. The coming and going of keeping accounts and currency conversions was very cumbersome. The Ministry of Finance will thoroughly abolish the unit of silver tael, otherwise it is impossible to recast all these existing silver taels into silver coins. However, it will take a great quantity to do so, hence, it needs to have detailed investigation, so that the statistics may come forth. Currently the number of silver bullions held by various banks and pawnshops, according to Chairman Lin Kanghou of the Bank Association, the total amount of silver bullions in circulation in the city is about 130 million taels.

British Merchant Ship Sinks Ningbo Merchant Ship

Crew Member Xia Yilin Drowned

The Ningbo fishing boat Ni Shunmao, loaded with sand and mud, came to Shanghai. On the 18th of this month, at approximately 5:00 AM, after unloading the sand and mud at Yangshupu, it sailed towards Ningbo. At 5:15 AM, while sailing on the Zhanghuabang River, it was struck by the British merchant ship G. Beniller, owned by Jardine Matheson & Co., which was sailing head-on without sounding its horn. Unable to avoid the collision, the Ningbo ship was hit on the beam, and the foremast broke immediately. Crew member Xia Yilin was knocked into the water by the broken mast.

The British ship, after hitting the Ni ship and seeing the crew member fall into the water, did not provide assistance but continued sailing towards Shanghai. Fortunately, the Zhanghuabang Customs patrol boat noticed the incident and immediately went to rescue the Ni ship, which did not sink. However, crew member Xia Yilin was severely injured and died shortly after being rescued.

It is reported that boatswain He Guisheng has sent a crew member, Xiao Man, back to his hometown to report to the boat owner, Ni Mingde, in preparation for filing a claim with the shipping company.

All Workers at the Two Railways' Wusong Machine Factory Go on Strike

Demanding the Dismissal and Investigation of General Affairs Director Mo Heng

Various Party Branches and Sub-Offices Rise Up in Support

The Management Bureau Holds Meetings for Several Days and Sends Personnel to Inspect the Factory

Since Huang Boqiao became the director of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, he transferred Mo Heng, the former section chief of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works, to serve as the director of general affairs. Conflicts have arisen frequently, especially the rejection of the contracting system by the loading and unloading workers at Maigen Road and the salary increase case in 1933.

The employees of the two railways have long been dissatisfied with Mo Heng's improper actions, his abuse of power, his slander of the Party and the country, and his disruption of the labor movement. They have endured these actions due to the national crisis. This time, Mo Heng was also appointed as the director of the materials department. He suddenly transferred Cao Wenkui (an clerk in the Wusong Materials Factory), the executive secretary of the Wusong Machine Factory branch of the two railways' labor union, to Ningbo.

Mo Heng stated to Mr. Cao that all those who participate in party affairs and the labor movement are dangerous elements, so he was transferring him to protect him. This has caused great dissatisfaction among the employees of the two railways, especially at the Wusong Machine Factory. The workers at the factory have now gone on strike, vowing to drive out Mo Heng.

They have issued a declaration to drive out Mo Heng, posted slogans throughout the stations, and submitted reports to the Central Executive Committee, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Railways, the party branches of the two railways, the management bureau of the two railways, and the labor union of the two railways, requesting the dismissal and investigation of Mo Heng. They have also sent telegrams to various parties for assistance. The information obtained is recorded below:

Declaration to Drive Out Mo Heng

Declaration by all workers of the Wusong Machine Factory of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways to drive out Mo Heng, Director of General Affairs and Director of Materials Department.

Fellow workers of the two railways, compatriots of the whole country! We know that the personnel serving in the railway public utility have important positions and receive good treatment. We can only strive to increase productivity and improve operations in order to live up to the country's desire for construction and maintain the stability of our personal lives. We also know that the only way out for the Republic of China is to implement the Three Principles of the People. Anyone who betrays the Chinese Kuomintang and hinders the implementation of the Three Principles of the People is undoubtedly a counter-revolutionary and must be sanctioned.

Unfortunately, since Mo Heng became the Director of General Affairs of the two railways, he has abused his power, acted perversely, deceived workers, and provoked discord in an attempt to achieve his own goals through despicable means. Recently, he also became the Director of the Materials Department, further increasing his power and threatening everyone. In order to protect the Party and the country, the labor union, railway property, and the interests of workers, we vow to drive out Mo Heng, the Director of General Affairs and Director of the Materials Department, who betrays the Party, pursues private interests, sabotages the labor movement, and endangers railway property.

The charges against him are briefly stated as follows, for the reference of all workers of the two railways and compatriots of the whole country:

(1) Pursuing private interests and engaging in corruption: The state-owned railways are the lifeline of the country. The two railways, which connect the capital, are even more important. All employees, especially senior officials, should economize on public funds and serve faithfully. However, Mo Heng is blinded by greed. He privately exchanges material purchase contracts with merchants and buys inferior goods at high prices. Fearing that his black deeds would be exposed, he transferred Zhang Zhiyun, the chief of the accounting section of the materials factory. The facts are clear and can be verified. It is inconceivable that such a crazy person would exist in an agency under a clean government, using public office for private gain and engaging in corruption. If this plague is not eliminated, the railway will be difficult to manage. We will never allow him to remain in a high position in the two railways to mislead the country and harm the workers.

(2) Betraying the Party and the country: Mo Heng is a civil servant under the rule of the National Government, but he harbors deep hatred for the Chinese Kuomintang. He always treats the Party as the most taboo topic and openly propagates to the employees of the two railways. If we are not forgetful, we should remember his profound slanders of party rule at Jiaxing Zhakou and Ningbo. Recently, he has intensified his actions and regards those who participate in party affairs and the labor movement as dangerous elements. His thoughts, words, and actions are all counter-revolutionary. Revolutionaries and counter-revolutionaries cannot coexist. It is the duty of loyal comrades to overthrow counter-revolutionaries.

(3) Sabotaging the labor movement: Supporting labor is a consistent policy of the Kuomintang. Strengthening the workers' organization is an urgent need for the workers. The labor union of the two railways has existed for several years, but Mo Heng has always refused to recognize the union. He refuses to accept any reports submitted by employees in the name of the labor union, or orders them to talk in a personal capacity. Recently, he suddenly transferred Cao Wenkui, an employee of the Wusong Materials Factory, to Ningbo. This is originally a routine matter of the railway administration, but the motive for his transfer is that Mr. Cao is currently the executive secretary of the Wusong Machine Factory branch and is very active in party affairs. In order to restrict the development of party affairs and the labor movement, Mo Heng transferred Mr. Cao and told him that participating in party affairs and the labor movement are dangerous actions. It can be seen that his sabotage of the labor movement is premeditated and has been going on for more than a day.

His crimes are certainly not limited to these, but these points are enough to illustrate the rest. For the sake of loving the Party, the country, the railway, and the workers, we will not stop until we achieve the goal of driving out Mo Heng. We want to retain Comrade Cao Wenkui to continue to be responsible for the Wusong Machine Factory branch. But we absolutely guarantee to abide by order and will never go beyond the rules. We hope that those who sympathize with us will provide assistance. This is our declaration.

Strike Situation

After the above facts occurred, all the workers of the Wusong Machine Factory and the Materials Factory immediately requested the Party branch and the labor union of the two railways to take action regarding the retention of Comrade Cao Wenkui and the absurdity of Director Mo's remarks. The Party branch dispatched members Chen Chengshi, Zou Kexin, and Li Dasan, and the labor union dispatched directors Min Luo Bing and Chen Bohua to negotiate with the railway bureau, but to no avail. Therefore, on the 19th, the workers of the two factories went on strike, vowing to drive out Mo Heng and carry out their original intention. The Party branch and the labor union are now doing their best to persuade and mediate in an attempt to prevent the dispute from escalating.

Support from All Sides

After receiving the telegram and declaration from the Wusong Machine Factory, the Party branches at all levels and the sub-offices and direct branches of the labor union of the two railways, based on past experiences and current events, for the sake of loving the Party, the country, the railway, and the workers, supporting the labor union, and protecting the interests of the workers, have risen up in support. For example, the first district party branch, the first, second, fourth, fifth, and sixth sub-branches of the first district, and the Shanghai Machine Factory sub-office have all issued declarations and telegrams separately, and have requested the Party branch of the two railways to forward them to the central government, demanding the dismissal and investigation of Mo Heng in order to appease the public.

Bureau Meeting

After learning that all the workers of the Wusong Machine Factory and the Materials Factory were on strike, the management bureau of the two railways immediately convened a meeting of the persons in charge of the general affairs, mechanical affairs, and materials departments to discuss countermeasures. On the previous two days, they sent Deputy Director of General Affairs Yuan Boyang, Director of Mechanical Affairs Wang Bi, Deputy Director of Mechanical Affairs and Director of the Chemical Experiment Institute Lu Baogang, and Liu Junming, a staff member of the Personnel Section, to Wusong to persuade the workers to resume work and wait for a solution. However, the workers were unanimously determined and unmoved.

Traffic Unimpeded

The New Voice News Agency reported that since the workers of the Wusong Machine Factory went on strike, all work at the factory has completely stopped. However, the employees of the two railways, as well as the workers of the Shanghai Machine Factory, Zhakou Machine Factory, and Baisha Machine Factory, are working as usual. Therefore, passenger and freight trains on the two railways are still running as usual without any impact. As for the repair of vehicles, the railway bureau has sent personnel to transport them to the Zhakou Machine Factory for repair. However, the repair of machinery will be temporarily handled by the Shanghai Machine Factory.

Mo Heng Resigns

The railway bureau believes that the transfer of Cao Wenkui, an employee of the Wusong Materials Factory, is within the administrative authority of the railway bureau and will continue to persuade the workers. As for Mo Heng, the director of general affairs and director of the materials department, it is reported that he has submitted a request to the director yesterday to send personnel to thoroughly investigate the truth in order to uncover the truth, and has also submitted his resignation. Directors Huang Boqiao and Wu Shaozeng believe that Mo Heng's transfer of personnel was carried out under orders and should be sincerely retained.
