Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegram to the Executive Yuan Urging Thorough Investigation of the Qinlian Soil Sugar Penalty Case

Reviving National Sugar Requires Protecting Existing Industries

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry (titles omitted): "On the 18th of this month, we received a letter from the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce of Guangdong Province stating: 'It is noted in the letter from the Qinlian Sugar Industry Guangyi Hall that we received letters from our fellow traders Heli, Henghe, Longguang, Changhe, and Heyi stating that from July to September of this year, these traders shipped native white sugar from Beihai to Shanghai five times. Each time, they reported to the Beihai Customs for inspection, confirming that it was pure native sugar. They paid the transit tax according to regulations and were then released. Unexpectedly, when the original cargo arrived in Shanghai, it was completely detained by the Jianghai Customs Tax Office, which claimed that it was mixed with 10% to 20% foreign sugar. A total of 1,560 yuan was fined, and 1,957 yuan was added to the tax. The method used to distinguish between native sugar and foreign sugar was without any standard, and many mistakes were made. The traders have already jointly submitted a petition and telegram to protest, but more than a month has passed, and the matter has not been resolved. The traders have suffered a significant loss innocently, forcing them to temporarily suspend business and await relief. A detailed list of the fined firms is specially provided for your review. We earnestly request that you forward the letter to the Beihai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Qinlian County Chambers of Commerce, who will report the situation to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, instructing the Jianghai Customs Tax Office to refund the fines in full to demonstrate fairness.' We have investigated that Beihai is an important port for the export of native sugar in South China. The Beihai Customs is close to the sugar-producing area and has a clear understanding of the composition of native sugar and its differences from foreign sugar. Therefore, our fellow traders have repeatedly reported the attached native sugar, which was inspected and released without any misunderstanding or difficulty. Now, the original cargo has been shipped directly to Shanghai, and the Jianghai Customs claims that it is mixed with foreign sugar and imposes a huge fine, which is obviously an abuse of power and a destruction of local products. If this is not stopped according to law, how can farmers and businessmen live in peace? We have specially recorded the case and presented it to you, earnestly requesting that you forward the letter according to the situation, so as to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants." The council approved this. Since the Jianghai Customs detained and fined native sugar, sugar merchants have ceased shipping, resulting in considerable losses. More than ten counties of farmers and workers who rely on the sugar industry for their livelihoods are at risk of bankruptcy and unemployment. Livelihoods and public security are greatly affected. Based on the aforementioned letter, and considering that the matter concerns the livelihoods of farmers and merchants in more than ten counties, we have specially joined with the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce to convene a public meeting of fellow traders, guilds, and all sugar merchants to discuss relief measures. Four resolutions were jointly agreed upon: (1) Request the Ministry of Finance to correct the erroneous methods of Jianghai Customs for distinguishing between native sugar and foreign sugar. (2) Request the Ministry of Finance to order Jianghai Customs to release the native sugar of Beihai sugar merchants and refund all previous fines and tax supplements. (3) Request the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Finance to instruct all customs offices nationwide to ensure the safety of native sugar imports and exports and not to deliberately create difficulties. (4) Request the central government to issue a clear order to exempt native sugar from export and transit taxes and to establish export incentive measures for native sugar. All were unanimously approved. In addition to telegrams and separate reports, we have specially recorded the case and jointly presented it to your association, and have sent representative Pang Songhui to explain everything in person. Please provide practical assistance so that this case can be resolved as soon as possible, which would not only be fortunate for the Qinlian sugar merchants but also for the entire national commerce." It was also reported that the native sugar from Qiong was transferred and exported, and the Qionghai Customs and Jianghai Customs referred to it as adulterated foreign sugar and detained it for punishment, involving as many as eight companies. The reading time was as long as seven months, and the association and the sugar merchants' representative Xing Juefei separately presented it to the hospital and the ministry, requesting arbitration and snow removal, but it has not been resolved so far. According to the previous report, Qinlian native sugar was transferred to Shanghai, and there was a continuous fine from the Shanghai Customs, which is even more frightening. The value of foreign sugar is higher than that of native sugar, and there is no reason to mix it with native sugar for sale, and foreign sugar transit is not required to pay taxes according to regulations, and there is no mixing with native sugar, which increases the amount of native sugar and voluntarily pays one more transit tax. Qiong sugar transit has been repeatedly confiscated and punished, and merchants operate safely, and there is no repeated sacrifice of blood capital, willing to risk the law. All of these situations have been repeatedly submitted to the hospital and the ministry for hosting and snow removal, but to this day, the destruction of customs officials remains the same, and its scope has expanded from Qiongyai to Qinlian, as if all sugar-producing areas in China are places where foreign sugar is smuggled and sold. This kind of arbitrary decision is already frightening. If that is the case, then the customs has already committed a major dereliction of duty. Whether foreign sugar is smuggled and sold is one thing, and whether native sugar is mixed and sold is another. Mixing high-priced foreign sugar with low-priced native sugar not only reduces the value, but also risks huge deductions and fines. Even the most foolish person would not do this. The output of domestic sugar is only counted by Sichuan and Guangdong. Now, Sichuan sugar is hindered from foreign sales due to the heavy taxes in the province, and Guangdong sugar is intentionally destroyed by customs officials, causing sugarcane farmers and sugar merchants there to be discouraged and create opportunities for foreign sugar to sell well, which is especially indignant. I have repeatedly read reports that the Ministry of Industry has a plan to revitalize national sugar, and the articles are well-organized and convincing. I implore you to first protect the existing industries before it can be effective. If Guangdong sugar is hindered everywhere when it is transshipped to various provinces, the gardeners and merchants will stop their business and change their plans, and the foundation of national sugar will be destroyed, and how can it be revitalized? Because of deep worries, the words are not so concise. Please ask the members of the hospital and the ministry to verify, and together with the repeated complaints about the Qiong sugar fines, quickly grant snow removal together, so that sugar merchants who are suppressed by customs officials can still see justice in the government. The eager hope is to comfort the public. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, kowtow, Xiao.

Escaped from Majiang and Xiaojiang

According to the Guowen News Agency, the naval Qingyun surveying vessel was previously hammering and measuring in Majiang. The Min Incident suddenly occurred, and the Changmen Fortress was taken over by the 19th Route Army, and it was impossible to escape for a while. At the same time, there were also two surveying vessels, Jingxing and Haigou, detained by Min. Now the Qingyun surveying vessel has escaped and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, led by Captain Zheng Tici, and is berthed at Gaochangmiao Port. In the afternoon, the reporter met with the personnel of the vessel, who said that they did not know anything about the Min Incident. When the Changmen Fortress was captured, the ship sailed to the upper reaches of Majiang. Jingxing and Haigou were in Mawei, so they were intercepted by the 19th Route Army, and all personnel were imprisoned. After the ship sailed to the upper reaches, it was learned that although the Changmen Fortress was taken over, it was difficult to pass through. However, there was still a Xiaojiang that could bypass the fortress and enter the sea. It was then confirmed that the Min side had not sent troops to guard it. Therefore, it took a detour through the port and escaped to Shanghai. There was no loss of personnel or any surveying equipment, which was really fortunate. Now Captain Zheng Tici has arrived in Shanghai and reported to Chen Tongling (Jiliang). He has already taken a car to Beijing last night.

Jin Xi's Family Representatives Petitioned the Municipal Government Again Yesterday

According to the Eurasia News Agency, Jin Xi, who has been naturalized and enrolled in school, was illegally arrested by the Japanese consulate in the French Concession. Yesterday afternoon, around 4 p.m., Jin Xi's family representatives, Chen Yang and others, stated that Jin has been arrested and detained for 29 days. According to Japanese law, the consulate cannot detain a prisoner for more than this number of days. If he is not released on time, he will be sent back to the country for processing. Therefore, they feel that Jin's future is extremely dangerous, and Jin's family is in a miserable and impoverished situation. Therefore, they met with Secretary Guo on behalf of the secretary. After Chen and Zhou expressed their intentions, Secretary Guo replied that the municipal government has already sent personnel to negotiate with the Japanese consul orally and formally protested in writing to demand his return based on reports from all parties and the request of Jin's family. Now the Japanese consul has replied, but the wording is extremely evasive, saying that the country has long had a clear order that Koreans are not allowed to transfer to any nationality, so they cannot recognize Jin's naturalization in your country. As for the French consulate, it has also requested the Japanese consul to return him according to law based on the concession agreement. Later, Chen, the family representative of Jin, asked him to forward to Mayor Wu the reasons for refuting the Japanese consul, saying that regarding the Japanese refusal to allow Koreans to transfer to other countries, it can be based on Jin Xi and his father Yongduo being arrested by the Japanese consul on November 30 last year. Fortunately, various groups negotiated with the Japanese consul to release him because Jin had been naturalized in China, which can prove that naturalization is not a problem. Now the municipal government is collecting various reasons to discuss the issue of refuting, and will submit a second protest to the Japanese consul within a few days.

Civil Servant Disciplinary Meeting Resolves That Xi Dejiong Did Not Falsify Engineering Reports

The General Situation Table of the River Embankment was Temporarily Made for Reference

The Qikou Embankment and Other Works Were Not Yet Accepted During the Flood

The Supervisory Yuan previously impeached Xi Dejiong, director of the Engineering Office of the National Economic Committee, for falsifying engineering reports and wasting huge sums of money. It decided to send him to the Central Civil Servant Disciplinary Committee for disciplinary action. The facts on which the Supervisory Yuan based its decision were the insufficient height of the Qikou Embankment and the dangerous situation of the Mahua Embankment. Xi was the director of the Engineering Office of the Flood Relief Committee after the flood in the 20th year of the Republic of China and was responsible for the construction of the main embankments of the Jianghuai Han Canal. After the Flood Relief Committee ended, the Engineering Office of the Economic Committee took over, and he was always in charge of the embankment work. He could not shirk his responsibility. After being transferred to the Central Civil Servant Disciplinary Committee, the committee investigated and found that the General Situation Table of the River Embankment, on which the supervisory committee members based their decision, was made by the Engineering Office this summer at the request of the Yangtze River Flood Prevention Association for reference. It was hastily made and incomplete and cannot be used as a formal basis. It decided to notify the Engineering Office of the Economic Committee that the Qikou Embankment and other places were contracted by the Chinese and Foreign Volunteer Relief Association and were only reported to be completed in March of this year and have not yet been accepted. It is not a formal report and cannot be considered as falsifying engineering reports and held responsible. As for the dangerous situation of the Mahua Embankment, the Jianghuai embankments under its management have a total length of more than 9,000 li. Due to weather, human affairs, economy, wind and rain erosion, tidal surge and other factors, this smallest part has sunk due to pressure, which is not intentional falsification.

The Yellow Disaster Relief Association Adds 100,000 Sets of Cotton Clothes

40,000 Sets for Hebei, 30,000 Sets for Henan, and 30,000 Sets for Shandong

The Distribution of 30,000 Yuan of Relief Grain to Various Counties in Henan is Resolved

The Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee added 100,000 sets of cotton clothes for women and children. 10,000 sets were contracted by the Shandong Houde Poor People's Factory. The remaining 90,000 sets were solicited for quotations by the Procurement and Transportation Group in Shanghai, and the three companies with the lowest prices were contracted. 13 pounds of blue cloth were used for the surface, 11 pounds of white cloth for the lining, and 2.5 liang of top white cotton for each set. The price for each set of women's clothing is 1.9002 yuan, and the price for each set of children's clothing is 1.1558 yuan. It is heard that they can be made ready soon and shipped out in a few days. It is estimated that there will be 40,000 sets for Hebei, 30,000 sets for Henan, and 30,000 sets for Shandong. In addition, the group recently issued 30,000 yuan of relief grain to Henan, and the Provincial Disaster Relief Committee decided to distribute the amount to the counties as follows: 10,200 yuan for Hua County, 2,000 yuan for Wen County, 2,000 yuan for Wuzhi, 2,000 yuan for Fengqiu, 2,000 yuan for Lanfeng, 2,000 yuan for Kaocheng, 1,000 yuan for Kaifeng, 1,000 yuan for Mengjin, 1,000 yuan for Meng County, 700 yuan for Shangqiu, 700 yuan for Shaanxi County, 600 yuan for Chenliu, 600 yuan for Zheng County, 600 yuan for Lingbao, 600 yuan for Qinyang, 500 yuan for Guangwu, 500 yuan for Sishui, 500 yuan for Zhongmou, 500 yuan for Minquan, 500 yuan for Gong County, 500 yuan for Yu County. In addition, 1,080 sets of cotton relief clothes that were previously left undistributed have now been allocated to the two reception centers, 540 sets each.

New Regulations on Domestic Chinese Telegram Charges by the Ministry of Communications

Implemented from the First Day of the New Year of the 23rd Year

New Rules for International Telegrams Will Also Be Changed at That Time

The Ministry of Communications has revised the regulations for domestic Chinese telegram charges, which will be implemented from January 1. At the same time, international telegrams will be changed according to the new Madrid rules. The following is an exploration of the various methods:

Time of Delivery The Ministry of Communications has issued the following instructions on the time of delivery: "To be viewed by all bureaus and stations, after this, social telegrams received before 8:00 should be delivered after 8:00, and those received after 21:00 should be delivered after 8:00 the next day. Please abide by this order."

Calculation Method The ministry has revised the calculation method for Chinese telegrams as follows: (1) The name of the receiving location and the name and address of the recipient of the above telegrams, not exceeding 15 characters, will be charged as 5 characters. If this is exceeded, the characters will be charged as before. (2) If a telephone number is used instead of the address, the recipient's name and the name of the receiving location will be calculated as a total of 4 characters. (3) Registered addresses and the names of receiving locations will still be charged according to previous regulations. (4) For telegrams sent separately, each additional recipient's name and address will be charged 3 characters. If the address is replaced by a telephone number, 2 characters will be charged. (5) Various fees and business identifications will be charged separately according to regulations. In addition, Chinese and foreign urgent telegrams to and from China should be charged at twice the ordinary telegram rate. The above methods will be implemented from January 1 next year.

Shanghai-Macau Retransmission The receiving and dispatching offices of the Great Northern, Great Eastern, Pacific, and other submarine cable companies have been recovered by our country and should be handled accordingly. It is necessary to consider whether this is applicable to Shanghai-Macau retransmission. A special order was issued to the International Telecommunication Bureau stating, "In order to facilitate public communication, the methods have been revised as follows. Please instruct the Great Northern and Great Eastern submarine cable telegram receiving and dispatching offices to comply." Whether the above method of calculating the recipient's name and address for Chinese telegrams is applicable to Shanghai-Macau telegrams and domestic telegrams transmitted by the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable, and whether the submarine cable fee for domestic urgent telegrams transmitted by the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable is reduced to twice the ordinary telegram rate, please contact and report separately.

International Telegrams For international telegrams, the new Madrid rules will be applied from January 1. The instructions stated, "To all bureaus, Hong Kong bureaus, and Guangdong-Guangxi bureaus and stations, the points where the new Madrid International Telegram Rules differ from the current rules have been summarized in a list by the International Telecommunications Bureau and distributed to each bureau and station. All foreign telegrams to and from China should be subject to the provisions of these new rules from January 1 next year. However, domestic coded telegrams will still be charged at full price, and each telegram will be limited to 5 characters. There is no need to add the (ODE) characters in the header. Please comply with this order."

More Than 60 Proposals for the Congress

26 from the Shanghai Medical Association, 3 from the Nanjing Medical Association, 1 from the Wuhu Medical Association, 2 from the Jiangyin Medical Association, 5 from the Hankou Medical Association, 2 from the Wujin Medical Association, 1 from the Jiangdu Medical Association, 1 from the Jinsha Medical Association, 3 from the Taixing Medical Association, 1 from the Huaining Medical Association, 2 from the Yin County Medical Association, 1 from the Shaoxing Medical Association, 3 from the Yunnan Kunming Medical Association, 3 from the Wu County Medical Association, 1 from the Wujiang County Medical Association, 3 from the Guangzhou Medical Association, 2 from the Qingdao Medical Association, and 3 from the Hangzhou Medical Association, totaling more than 60 items. It is also stipulated that the receipt of proposals will be stopped immediately. Later cases will not be considered as temporary proposals, and the following detailed rules are stipulated:

Detailed Regulations for the General Assembly

"Regulations for Deliberation," (1) This conference is scheduled to be convened in Nanjing on January 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of the 23rd year of the Republic [1934]; (2) Before the meeting, the secretary of this association shall inform each member of all known proposals and reports; (3) When the meeting is in session, the presidium shall act as the chair. The presidium shall be elected by the preparatory meeting; (4) This meeting shall have a quorum of more than half of the registered members. The designated representatives of each member organization shall be the attending members. Members outside of the designated representatives, and formal physicians from physician organizations in various locations, shall be non-voting members; (5) Various proposals shall be passed by the approval of more than half of the attending members; (6) Non-voting members shall only have the right to offer opinions and shall have no voting rights; (7) When the meeting is in session, the Department of Health or local health administrative authorities may attend to express their opinions; (8) These regulations shall be implemented after being passed by the preparatory meeting. "Regulations for Proposals," (1) Proposals from domestic physicians or medical organizations must be sent two weeks before the general assembly (individual proposals must also be submitted by organizations); (2) After receiving a proposal, this association shall immediately submit it to the proposal committee for review and incorporation into the agenda; (3) Before the meeting, the secretary of this association shall notify each member of the various proposals; (4) After the chair presents a proposal during the meeting, they may ask the proposer to explain the reasons (if the proposer is not present, they may entrust someone to represent them), but the explanation shall not exceed five minutes; (5) After the proposer explains the reasons, the chair shall submit it to the public for discussion; (6) During the discussion, each member must apply in order and speak only after being permitted by the chair. Each person shall not exceed five minutes; (7) After the discussion, the chair shall put it to a vote, and it shall be passed by the approval of more than half of the attending members. Regulations for Emergency Proposals (1) If there are any emergency proposals at this meeting, the following regulations shall apply; (2) Emergency proposals must be submitted by member organizations and must be countersigned by more than two attending organizations; (3) Emergency proposals must be submitted to the presidium in printed form twelve hours before the meeting for review and decision; Emergency proposals shall be listed after the original proposals; (5) After the presidium announces an emergency proposal, the proposer shall explain the reasons, but the explanation shall not exceed five minutes; (6) After the proposer explains the reasons for an emergency proposal, it must be voted on by more than half of the attending members before it can be established and discussed; (7) During the discussion of an emergency proposal, each member must apply in order and speak only after being permitted by the chair. Each person shall not exceed five minutes; (8) After the discussion, the chair shall put it to a vote, and it shall be passed by the approval of more than half of the attending members. The dates for the general assembly to host representatives from various locations have also been set.

Date and Location for General Assembly Reception

A reception center will be set up at the Central Hotel in Daxing Palace, Nanjing, starting from the 30th of this month, and will begin operations. Notices have been sent to member organizations in various locations, inviting attending and non-voting representatives to register on time. The public is also welcome to observe during the conference. It is expected that the capital will be bustling at that time.

Liang Shichun Returns from Europe and America and Discusses Observations on World War II

Says Conflict Between Russia and Japan is Inevitable

It is Almost Impossible for Us to Maintain Strict Neutrality

Liang Shichun, an executive of the National YMCA, was previously tasked with traveling to Europe and America for research. He has now returned to Shanghai from the United States on the President Hoover. According to Liang's travels in Europe and America, and the results of his talks with foreign dignitaries, he deeply feels that the conflicts of interest between countries are becoming increasingly acute, and war clouds are densely packed internationally. The seriousness of the situation exceeds that of 1914. According to Liang's personal speculation, the second

World War

is about to break out soon. When Liang arrived in Shanghai, he made the following remarks to reporters from various newspapers. Liang said, "If we observe from a factual perspective, the precariousness of our current position is unprecedented in history. The secret expansion of armaments by various countries and the intensity of their rivalry far surpass that of 1914. In addition, the rise of nationalism and the panic of the world economy are enough to promote the opening of World War II." Liang believes that the outbreak of World War II will

Definitely be in the Far East

Because recently, Russia and Japan have been making every effort to build railways in Siberia that have no commercial value. Their purpose is nothing more than to facilitate the transportation of troops to the war zone when the war breaks out. Although the recent recognition of Soviet Russia by the United States has given Japan a great threat, preventing the war from happening for a while, this move cannot eliminate the root cause of the conflict between Russia and Japan. Soviet Russia has no intention of war because its domestic construction has not been completed, but Japan is the opposite. Japan is deeply afraid that after the completion of Soviet Russia's construction, its national power will inevitably become stronger, which will make Japan feel even more inconvenient. At the same time, the Japanese military is extremely eager

to fight Russia

in order to complete its power in Manchuria as soon as possible. Therefore, the outbreak of World War II is feared to be imminent. Liang also said that after the outbreak of the Russo-Japanese War, China should take an attitude of strict neutrality in my personal opinion, but I am deeply afraid that strict neutrality is virtually impossible. It is also heard that Liang once represented China at the Fifth Pacific National Relations Discussion Conference. While in Europe and the United States, he met with U.S. Secretary of State Hull, U.S. Ambassador to Europe Davis, Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson, French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, and other international diplomatic figures. Therefore, his experience is very rich, and his observations are worthy of our reference.

The Second Police District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau Changes the Use of Garbage Bins in Its Territory

From January 15th of Next Year

Public Bins Will Be Discontinued, and Businesses Will Prepare Their Own Bins

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security and Health Bureaus, in view of the fact that the city's sanitation and cleaning matters have not presented a special effect, are due to the fact that citizens do not pour garbage into the bins. In order to rectify the city appearance, it was presented to the municipal government for approval, and it was decided that from January 15th, 23rd year of the Republic [1934], the public garbage bins originally set up in the territory under the jurisdiction of the Second District and Second Station will be discontinued. Each store will prepare its own garbage bin according to its capacity, and the sanitation bureau's scavengers will go to collect and transport it on time every day, so as to avoid arbitrary dumping and maintain the cleanliness of the roads. Yesterday, a joint announcement was issued, ordering all households, stores, etc. to quickly prepare garbage bins before the 25th of this month to facilitate implementation.

Attention to Those Who Need Saltpeter and Sulfur

Announcement No. 5 of the Northern Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Saltpeter and Sulfur Bureau of the Ministry of Finance: For the purpose of announcement, it is hereby noted that saltpeter and sulfur are important military supplies, so the state has established a bureau to monopolize sales to prevent harm and enrich the tax treasury, and to facilitate merchants and people. All merchants and households who need saltpeter and sulfur, such as fireworks, "silver work," "hunting," "incense industry," "cured meat," "chemical industry," "leather workshop," and other industries, are within the scope of the exclusive sales of this branch. They should all go to No. 1, Lane 1, Qiu'an Li, Meiyuan Road, Zhabei, to purchase according to the amount required. There must be no abuses such as "private hawking," "private wholesaling," "cross-border sales," and "peddling." Those who deliberately violate this will be punished according to the law. For fear of not knowing everything, this announcement is hereby made, so that all should abide by it and not violate it. Sincerely, Gu Xie, Director, December 18, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

A Guangdong Youth Dies by Poisoning

A Guangdong youth, surnamed Zhang, 25 years old, used to work in a factory on Nanjing Road. However, because he liked to play and spend money like water, his brother found out and transferred him to work in a factory on Zhejiang Road. Before long, he was transferred back, but economic sanctions were imposed. Zhang felt depressed and unhappy in his heart, and the idea of suicide arose. At 12 o'clock the night before, he returned from the outside and secretly took a heavy dose of medicine and committed suicide. At 11 o'clock the next morning, he had not yet gotten up. His brother entered the room to check and saw that his complexion was pale and he was unconscious. He hurriedly sent him to the Tongren Hospital by car. After the doctor gave him injections and medicine, but because he had taken too much poison, he eventually died after a while.

The Mastermind of the Assassination of Gu Daosheng Sentenced to Twenty Years in Prison

Gu Daosheng, a native of Dachang, 29 years old this year, was celebrating his father-in-law, Jin Luting's sixtieth birthday at the Dajilou Restaurant on Xiaodongmen Street in the French Concession on March 26 of this year. At about 3 pm that day, he was lured out on the pretext of delivering gifts and shot to death. Later, a Jiangbei native, Zhang Dianchen, was arrested by a French detective at the Oriental Hotel and sent to the Second Special District Court, where he was sentenced to life imprisonment. After appealing, the sentence was reduced to 15 years. Later, a French detective was dispatched to Changzhou, together with investigators from the Jiangsu Bandit Suppression Headquarters, and a Changzhou native, Zhang Jinbao, the mastermind of this case, was arrested in Yixing and transferred to Shanghai. A public prosecution was filed by the Second Special District Court. After Judge Li Changnian opened court several times to investigate the situation, which has been reported in previous newspapers, the trial has now concluded. Yesterday morning, Judge Li came to the First Criminal Court and sentenced Zhang Jinbao to 20 years of imprisonment for conspiring to commit murder. The number of days of detention before the final judgment was determined to be one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. The defendant was transferred to the detention center. After the judgment, Tang Hao, the lawyer defending Zhang, declared in court that he did not understand and requested an appeal. The court granted it.

Fire Broke Out in Ankang Lane Last Night

At about 11 o'clock last night, a fire broke out on the ground floor of the Wu family at No. 14, Ankang Lane, No. 315, at the corner of Yunnan Road and Jiujiang Road. The fire spread to the stairs, and the fire was blazing, and the situation was very fierce. The Central Fire Brigade rushed to rescue and gradually extinguished the fire at about 12 o'clock. A total of four single-story houses, Nos. 10, 12, 14, and 16, were burned down. Most of the residents in the lane were laborers, so they were all awakened from their sleep when the fire broke out and fled empty-handed, losing all their suitcases and belongings. Deng, a tenant on the upper floor of No. 14, was injured by jumping from the building and has been sent to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Water Supply to Tonghai Lane in Hongkou Cut Off the Day Before Yesterday

The Lives of All Residents Are in Imminent Danger

Representatives Will Be Sent to Petition the Municipal Council Today

The Reclamation Bank Announces the Process of Cutting Off Water

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the main pipe of Tonghai Lane, Tongzhou Road, Hongkou, in this city, was suddenly closed by the water company at 10 o'clock the day before yesterday, cutting off the water supply, causing the lives of all residents to be in imminent danger. The various situations obtained by the Xin Xin News Agency reporter are recorded below:

Petition to the Municipal Council Today

Tonghai Lane, Tongzhou Road, Hongkou, is managed by the Real Estate Department of the China Reclamation Bank. There are more than sixty houses in total, and the rent for each house is 26 yuan, and the rent for each shop is 34 yuan. The total number of residents is about 2,000, most of whom are poor. Now, in order to oppose the landlord's desire to increase the water bill during this economic depression (4 yuan per house), the water company suddenly closed the main pipe at 10 am yesterday, cutting off the water supply, causing thousands of residents to suddenly have no water to drink, causing great panic, and their lives were in imminent danger. They immediately convened all the residents to discuss countermeasures. As a result, Liu Zhenbo was appointed to petition the Municipal Council today, requesting assistance.

Reclamation Bank Announces the Process of Cutting Off Water

The Shanghai China Reclamation Bank Real Estate Department sent a letter to the Xin Xin News Agency yesterday, stating that the department has more than sixty houses in Tonghai Lane, Tongzhou Road, in the eastern district, with a monthly rent of about 1,600 yuan. Most of the residents are middle-class. Since the January 28th Incident, the economy has been depressed and life has been difficult. However, the British Shanghai Water Company secretly canceled the water package system in December of last year, installed water meters, and charged according to the meter, with monthly bills often between 550,000 and 1 million gallons, exceeding the water package system by about three times. This department followed the announcement of the Real Estate Association and temporarily paid according to the original price before the problem was resolved, but the company refused to accept it and threatened to cut off the water supply. Considering that there are nearly a thousand residents in the lane, once the water is cut off, wouldn't the lives and property of thousands of people be in a desperate situation? Therefore, in May, they went to the company to negotiate repeatedly and painfully paid 10% of the rent for water, which was already a large increase compared to the original price. Since May, the company has said that the water price has been revised, but it still exceeds the water package system by three or four times. Considering that the water consumption of the tiger stove and tofu shop is large, they did not hesitate to spend a lot of money to ask the company to dig up the road, re-drain the pipes, and install separate meters, which cost hundreds of yuan, and the water bill is still more than twice as much as the water package system. Just as they were about to collect it from the residents, the company suddenly closed the main pipe and cut off the water supply at 10 am on the 19th of this month. Thousands of residents are in imminent danger. Such actions, I think, will not only harm this department, but I hereby report to your newspaper and quickly ask to uphold justice in order to maintain the lives of the people.

Before Su San Was Escorted, Copper Chains Were Locked on Apprentices First

Gao Defu's Old Play Newly Made

Lu Huichun Was Innocent and Suffered

Lu Chen, a Tianjin woman residing at No. 64, Fengyu Lane, Route Sayzo, French Concession, 35 years old this year, is the wife of the late famous actor Lu Yueqiao. Ten years ago, she entrusted her son, Lu Huichun (17 years old this year), to Gao Defu (40 years old this year, a martial arts actor from Suzhou, currently living with Lu's wife at No. 56 in the same lane) to learn acting, learning civil and martial arts roles. Because Huichun had been away from home for a long time, he missed his mother very much. Because Gao was not there, he came to Shanghai alone from Jinan at the beginning of the month, and transferred to Suzhou. He arrived in Shanghai on the 18th of this month. He first went to Gao's place to meet him, and then explained to Gao that he wanted to go home to visit his mother. Gao not only refused, but also feared that he would go home privately, so he used a copper chain, the same one used in the play "Su San Escorted," to lock Huichun's hands and feet and confine him in a room in his home, not allowing him to make a sound. However, Huichun's mother, Lu Chen, although living nearby, did not know that her son had returned to Shanghai and was locked up by Gao. The news was spread by Gao's neighbors and detected by the French police, who sent a detective to Gao's house to investigate the day before yesterday. They found Huichun locked up in the room and unable to move freely. They arrested Gao and took Huichun to the police station. After the police chief questioned him, he ordered Gao to be detained. At the same time, he opened the chains for Huichun, informed his mother, and handed him over to be taken back. Yesterday, the police sent Gao to the Second Special District Court for questioning. The prosecutor, Fei Xizhen, said that the defendant had violated the crime of obstructing freedom under the criminal law. The police are currently investigating and have not concluded the investigation. He requested a postponement of the questioning. He also presented the chain as evidence. After reviewing the report in court and questioning the defendant, he was instructed to postpone the questioning until the 29th. The defendant was still detained in the detention center.

Rong paid him 300 yuan in cash and entrusted him to mediate. Unexpectedly, Xue received the money and there was no news for a long time. Rong suspected he had been cheated, so he hired a lawyer to apply for the license himself in order to open the business. A few days ago, he suddenly met Xue and asked about the license. Xue claimed that the 300 yuan had been given to the foreigner, but he thought the amount was too small, so it had not yet been approved, and he needed to add another 200 yuan to get it done. Rong Xinda and the witnesses also gave detailed accounts of the situation at the time. When asked, the defendant confessed: I only asked the plaintiff to give gifts, and the plaintiff gave me 300 yuan to pass on. Later, the foreigner refused to accept it, and I returned the money to the plaintiff that day. Qin Liansheng witnessed it. A few days ago, the plaintiff repeatedly asked me and sent 200 yuan. I had just received it when I was arrested. Bandits Forcibly Expel the Driver

Four Banks Preparatory Treasury Issues Preparatory Report

No. 207

The Four Banks Preparatory Treasury is jointly established by the Salt Industry Bank, Jincheng Bank, Zhongnan Bank, and Dalu Bank, specializing in issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. The issuance of banknotes is in accordance with the treasury's issuance regulations, with full preparation. Cash preparation is at least 60%, and guarantee preparation is at most 40%. It is announced once a week, and it is inspected by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The following is a record of the 207th announcement of the Shanghai Preparatory Treasury on December 16, 1933: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 28,484,237 yuan; Total amount of reserve: 28,484,237 yuan; including: Cash reserve: 22,481,987 yuan; Guarantee reserve: 6,002,250 yuan.

▲ "Diplomatic Review" Twelfth Issue: The twelfth issue of the second volume of "Diplomatic Review" has already been published. Several articles in this issue are worth reading, such as Wu Songgao's "Review of the World Crisis in 1936," which offers unique insights. First, it discusses the transfer of the mandated governance of Pacific islands, how to renew the London Naval Treaty after it expires in 1930, and the issue of the sovereignty of the Saar territory. Then, it compares the importance of the above three issues. Finally, it discusses the major changes in the future Pacific situation and China's influence and necessary preparations. Zhao Lanping's "Further Discussion on the American Economic Panic and Monetary Policy" reveals the direct cause of the run on American banks this spring and the special circumstances of the United States abandoning the gold standard, to show the difference between the suspension of the gold standard in the United States and Japan. It also evaluates the recent recovery movement and the policy of purchasing raw gold. Zhao Jiade's "New American Foreign Policy" is something we particularly want to know about. Since Roosevelt took office, the ambiguity of foreign policy has made people suspicious. The author lives in the United States, and reading this article will definitely reveal a glimpse of American foreign policy. Other articles, such as Yuan Daofeng's "Deterioration of Japanese-Russian Relations and China," and Shen Zhongmai's translation of "American-Russian Re-establishment of Relations in the Eyes of the Japanese," are all timely works.

Education News Outside Shanghai

He Chengjun Telegraphs Finance and Education Ministries to Promote Independent Education Funding in Hubei Province

▲ Education Department Orders Counties to Use Land Reclamation to Subsidize Education Funds

(Hankou Correspondence) The case for independent funding of education in Hubei Province, initiated by Education Director Cheng Qibao and supported by various schools and museums, has been approved by the provincial government and is certain to be implemented. The main points of the plan are that provincial and municipal funding will be independent at the same time. The provincial funds, from the central government's monthly allocation of 200,000 yuan, will be designated to be allocated monthly from the Hubei Customs Transport Bureau's salt tax. The Hankou municipal funds will be allocated from housing rent revenue. Both will be designated as special funds and are not allowed to be used for other purposes. The method of safekeeping is that each educational institution will form a safekeeping committee with various associations and jointly take responsibility. However, since the provincial funds are designated from the salt tax, it is appropriate to consult with the Finance and Education Ministries. In addition to requesting the provincial government to consult with the two ministries, Cheng Qibao also sent a letter to He Chengjun, the Pacification Commissioner stationed in Hubei, to find ways to promote its success. On the 17th, He sent a telegram to Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi and Education Minister Wang Shijie, stating, "Nanjing, Minister Kong, Yongzhi brother, Minister Wang, Xueting brother, I recently received a letter from Hubei Education Director Cheng Qibao stating that Hubei education funding has a precedent of being allocated from the salt tax surcharge. Now, in order to implement the above proposal, it has been proposed that 200,000 yuan be allocated monthly from the central government's allocation by the Hubei Customs Transport Bureau as a special fund for education in Hubei Province. This not only avoids the trouble of central remittance but also has the effect of nearby investigation and collection. The above measures and the regulations of the Education Fund Safekeeping Committee have been submitted to the provincial government for consultation with the Finance and Education Ministries for review. I urge you to send a special telegram to the central authorities to promote its success, etc. Hubei education is greatly affected due to the lack of special funding. When I was in the provincial government, I also once telegraphed the Yuanbu for a request. Now, according to the letter from the director, the various points are very insightful. I especially telegram the two brothers, hoping that you will consider the difficulties of Hubei education and grant the request. I am deeply grateful, He Chengjun." Cheng Qibao believes that Hubei's education is lagging behind, relying solely on this fund is not enough to promote its expansion, and each county's education funding is insufficient, so we must find ways to open up new sources. He further proposed three methods: (1) Most of the existing wasteland in various counties is unmanaged and regarded as waste. The county governments should order the district chiefs to conduct a thorough survey, list them, allocate them as academic property, and widely plant forests and suitable plants, as well as income to subsidize education funds. (2) There is a party fee surcharge in the county government donations of various counties. Now, after investigating that the party fees of various counties are directly issued by the central government, this surcharge should still be collected by the agent collecting the taxes and turned over to the educational administrative agencies of various counties for safekeeping as education funding. (3) For local major products, education donations may be appropriately collected, but it must be submitted to the county government and forwarded to the Department of Finance for the record, and it should be based on not being harsh or disturbing.

Dai Yingguan Inspects the General Situation of Education in Hebei and Peiping (2)

Dai Yingguan, Section Chief of the Ministry of Education, is inspecting the education in Hebei Province and Peiping. The situation of education in Hebei Province has been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the situation of education in Peiping is described below.

Education in Peiping is most developed at the middle school level. There are six municipal schools, and fifty-one private schools that have been registered. There is one municipal normal school, and one private kindergarten normal school attached to the Xiangshan Orphanage. There are only two municipal vocational schools and a vocational class attached to the orphanage. Peiping has many universities and independent colleges. The need for ordinary middle schools is greater than in general cities. However, what is needed are complete middle schools that can cultivate young people with the physical strength and intelligence to enter universities, and whose character is honest and whose thinking is correct. After entering university, they can continue to cultivate themselves and create various experts and national leaders. In this sense, Peiping still feels the lack of middle schools. Although I personally cannot conduct a universal inspection this time, I have generally inspected the public and private middle schools that are representative. Among them, the most profound impression is the Qiu Zhi Girls' Junior Middle School in Xizhimen. Ninety-five percent of the students in the school come from poor families. Their parents are either coolies, vendors, rickshaw pullers, or police officers. The remaining five percent have parents whose economic situation is about 50 yuan per month. The school does not charge students any fees. The school spirit is serious, and the teaching and labor courses are well-equipped. The funding is the responsibility of the school board. Mr. Feng Lidequan is especially enthusiastic in supporting it. Today's education in our country is almost entirely a privilege enjoyed by the rich and powerful. The League of Nations Education Observation Group has already spoken about it. Children from the lower classes are especially unlikely to enjoy middle school education. The establishment of this school is truly good news for poor girls. When Peiping's education circles talk about middle schools, they all praise the attached middle school of the Normal University. Judging from the scientific equipment and teaching situation of each subject, the attached middle school truly lives up to its name. The disadvantage of the school is that there are no student dormitories, which makes it difficult to implement the training spirit. However, the spirit of group training implemented by the school is already very significant. Judging from the equipment and teaching, Municipal No. 4 Middle School and Hebei Provincial Peiping High School are both good. Other schools, such as Yuanman Girls' Middle School's English teaching, group students according to ability in the same grade. The teachers' academic ability and skills are excellent. Yiwen Middle School, famous for implementing the Dalton Plan, has students learning in the workshops very sincerely and happily, and the results are quite impressive. Peiping has two middle schools with the most developed students, namely Zhicheng and Hongda. Each school has more than 1,500 students. Hongda has built quite neat school buildings. Zhicheng has purchased instruments and medicines worth 20,000 yuan, which are taken from the students and used for the students. Those who run private schools should be like this. The common disadvantage of the two schools is that each class has about 70 students, exceeding the regulations of the middle school curriculum, which makes teaching and training extremely difficult. Kongde Middle School has a considerable history. The students' behavior is lively and their Chinese language performance is quite good. However, after inspecting the teaching situation, the students' spirits are too lacking in vigor. There are even those who hide and lie down, and others who stare out the window, thinking that a swan is about to arrive. What is seen from the outside is like this, and it is difficult to say how concentrated their inner lives are on their studies. Peihua Girls' Middle School has very few students. When inspecting, the high school was lecturing on foreign history and foreign geography, using English texts. When asked how Chinese history and Chinese geography were taught, it was said that there was no Chinese history or Chinese geography in high school. There were two classes in its primary school that were lecturing on the Christian Bible. It was said that it was extracurricular homework, but it was clearly class teaching. Generally speaking, the shortcomings of general middle schools in Peiping are: (1) The school buildings are narrow, and most students are day students. (2) The library and science equipment are simple. (3) There is a lack of close contact between teachers and students, and it is difficult to give correct guidance to young people's thoughts and actions. (4) The teaching method is mostly lecture-style. (5) Labor education is mostly neglected. (6) Most of the textbooks for each subject have not been approved. (7) Students' absence records are not strictly checked. (8) Schools charge students too much fees. The kindergarten normal class and attached kindergarten jointly run by the orphanage and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau have mostly children from poor families. In the current education situation in our country, the poor only have the opportunity to receive primary school and supplementary education. Kindergarten education before middle school and kindergarten is purely a special privilege enjoyed by the rich and powerful. The kindergarten and the Qiu Zhi Girls' Middle School can be called the two major characteristics of Peiping education. The workers' department of the Tzu Institute is entered by graduates of primary schools. During the day, they work in factories, and at night, they still supplement their academic subjects. After three years of work, they are taught the theory of the subjects they have learned, which is a reform and experiment in running vocational education. The municipal vocational school and commercial school can both pay attention to practical training, but the school buildings are small and need to be expanded urgently. Among the universities specially inspected in Peiping, the Northeast University school buildings are divided into three parts, making administration and management difficult. The two colleges of science and engineering have no equipment and must borrow from the engineering college of Peiping University. The school's moral education is purely centered on military training. The students' actions can be called disciplined and their lives are used to hardship. The professors' treatment is no different from that of middle school teachers, but their spirit is excellent. There are many departments in Mingguo College. In the past, students were arbitrarily absent, but now they are actively rectifying it and strictly cracking down on students' absences. Peiping has a large number of schools, but only one section of the Social Affairs Bureau is in charge, and there are very few staff, so supervisors have no time to inspect the schools. Tianjin has a municipal education bureau as an ordinary city, and Qingdao, although a municipality directly under the central government and small in scope, also has an education bureau. Only Peiping, which had a supervision bureau since the Qing Dynasty, has now been abolished. If the municipal government's finances are strained, if it can plan comprehensively or save some of the money for entertaining guests every month, it will not be difficult to restore the Municipal Education Bureau. Only with a sound municipal education bureau can Peiping's education be discussed and rectified. (End)

Liangjiang Defeats Green Team

Although this match was relatively important, the chaotic situation made it less interesting. The Green Team's forwards were clumsy and their shooting skills were quite rudimentary. The defenders were better. Liangjiang's Chen Rongming was slightly lacking, while the forwards relied on Yang Sen's performance. The defenders were best represented by Chen Baixue. After the initial exchange, Yang Sen opened the scoring. The Green Team then scored a point through Han Mengte. After that, the two sides were evenly matched, with few scoring opportunities. The Green Team bravely shot but lacked the skill, leaving them frustrated. The first quarter ended in a 4-4 tie. From the first quarter onwards, Liangjiang's Xu Suifeng replaced Chen Rongming, and Yang Sen continued to score. The Green Team did not weaken, and the situation remained even. After 9-7, Chen Rongming re-entered, but the first half had already ended. After the break, Liangjiang worked hard to attack, and the Green Team resisted desperately. Neither side scored for a long time. Liangjiang then opened up a path and gradually improved, but before long, Pan Mengshi, Ruixia, and Chen Hongying were fouled out one after another. Therefore, in the final quarter, the Green Team tried to counter-attack, and Han Mengte made two free throws. Liangjiang was unwilling to let go, and in a final struggle, Liangjiang won 20-13. The referee was strict at first and then lenient, and tended to nitpick.

The Middle School Football Final: Pudong and Yuqing Battle to a Draw

1-1 = Each Team Scores One Goal in Each Half, After Extra Time, Both Sides Still Tied, Second Final Next Wednesday

Yesterday was the date of the Middle School Football Final. The elite troops of Pudong and Yuqing arrived on time. The cheering squads from both sides totaled no less than three or four hundred people, and the shouting was deafening. The situation was quite lively, and the offense and defense of both sides were evenly matched. The actions were also very peaceful and upright. Unfortunately, the coldness suddenly increased yesterday, and many athletes on the field suffered from muscle strains, which naturally affected their performance. The result was a 1-1 draw. Twenty minutes of extra time were added, but neither side gained anything. However, the spirit of struggling on the right track is enough to be admired by the Jiangda Football League. The battle situation is briefly recorded below:

▲Li Muyao Scores the Goal After Chen Jixiang blew the whistle to start the battle, the Pudong heroes immediately pressed aggressively into Yuqing's defense zone. Wu Jiugao repeatedly repelled the enemy's attack. Luo Douwen's long-legged kicks had the charm of Luo Haiguang. He opened fire from a distance, and his strength was amazing. It was a pity that the goal was short and the ball was high, so he could not score. Li Jinji summoned the three armies and invaded the south for the second time, like wolves and tigers, with great momentum. In an instant, they broke into the opponent's penalty area. Weng Kefa missed a kick, and Li Muyao rushed to kick and shoot directly into the goal. The Pudong support team was overjoyed and ecstatic.

▲Fu Zhibin Takes Revenge The Pudong formation is characterized by neatness, which is not easy to shake under any circumstances. In terms of talent, Yuqing's forwards are quite brave, but they are all brave men and cannot achieve anything. After Pudong scored a goal, the situation became more chaotic. After the break, Yuqing's instructor Zhang Zhizhen gave instructions, and things began to improve slightly. After holding on until 57 minutes, Yuqing's five forwards besieged Pudong's goal for a long time without success. Fu Zhibin was an veteran after all. At the 15-yard mark, he found a gap and shot, making it a tie.

▲After Extra Time Seventy minutes passed like a flash. Both sides scored a goal, so twenty more minutes were added to determine the winner. After exchanging defense zones, Yuqing's momentum was quite strong, but they repeatedly missed opportunities. In the first ten minutes, Pudong conserved its strength to defend, and Yuqing could only call in vain. In the last ten minutes, the defense zones were adjusted again, and most of the soldiers on both sides had muscle strains. They had no intention of fighting, and the score was 0-0 at the end of the game. It has now been decided to hold a second final next Wednesday.

Cheng Yize Hosts a Banquet to Celebrate the Chinese Race Walking Team's Achievements

Yesterday (the 19th) at 8:00 p.m., Cheng Yize, chairman of the Chinese Race Walking Association, hosted a banquet at his private residence on Matterhorn Road to celebrate the Chinese team's double championship. In addition to all the members of the Chinese race walking team, there were also Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, Yu Hengzhi, Shi Youhui, as well as the president of the International Race Walking Association, Mr. Littell, vice president McKenna, honorary secretary Mayfe, and more than fifty other people. Mr. Cheng personally greeted the guests with great hospitality, which was much admired. During the banquet, Mr. Cheng first stood up to give a speech, saying that he was very pleased that the Chinese race walking team had won the double championship again. He hoped that the athletes would maintain their past spirit, continue to maintain the championship, and bring glory to the country. He had prepared a simple meal tonight to celebrate, and he was also very honored that Hao Gengsheng, Shen Siliang, Littell, and McKenna had come to give guidance. After the speech, Mr. Littell and McKenna spoke one after another, expressing their admiration for the beautiful posture of the Chinese team members and hoping that they would win the championship every time. They also thanked the Chinese people for their assistance in making the event a success. Next, Hao Gengsheng and Shen Siliang gave speeches. The former mentioned that the government has recently paid great attention to sports, and that the Chinese race walking team has achieved such great results that it will definitely be able to win glory for the country on the world stage in the future. The latter gave a brief explanation of the Chinese team's participation in the competition with new players, and the Chinese Race Walking Association's preparations for participating in the 1936 World Games held in Germany. He also hoped that the athletes would practice actively and live up to their mission. He also praised Shi Youhui and Lu Yutian for their enthusiastic service and indispensable contributions. Mr. Shen also said that the sudden refusal of the racecourse to lend the venue for reasons was a great impact on Sino-foreign relations, and he deeply regretted the inappropriate measures taken by the racecourse. Finally, Shi Youhui stood up on behalf of the race walking team to thank Chairman Cheng for his enthusiastic promotion and repeated banquets. The atmosphere was lively and grand, and the banquet did not end until midnight.

A List of Surveys on National Arts Halls in Various Provinces and Cities

Since its establishment five years ago, the Central National Arts Hall has not been able to set up branch halls due to difficult funding. The establishment of National Arts Halls in various provinces and cities has now spread throughout the country. All funding is raised by the provinces and cities themselves. According to a person from the hall, a total of 25 places have been reported as established. Except for Jiangsu and Hubei provinces, which have been suspended, there are currently 23 places. Although the number of National Arts branch halls in various provinces and counties that have been established has not been surveyed in detail, it is estimated that there are no less than 300 in total, averaging ten counties per province. Among them, Qingdao City has the most, with 83 National Arts training centers, the most in the country's cities and districts. The survey results are listed below:

Shenbao National Products Weekly

Contributions

Alas, the Alarming Trade Deficit of 900 Million Yuan

— Yang An

The International Trade Bureau reported to the Ministry of Industry that the trade deficit for the first half of this year was over 474 million yuan, and it is estimated that the total for the year will be about 900 million yuan. Readers, please close your eyes and consider this alarming number. The trade deficit of a country increases year after year to this record high. This phenomenon has never been seen since the opening of trade. On average, each person must bear more than two yuan worth of foreign goods. How can this be ignored? I think that even if the Chinese people are numb and unfeeling, and unaware of the danger, they should be shocked and awakened when they see foreign goods flooding the market and domestic products shrinking. They should quickly find a countermeasure. There is no such thing as sitting back and waiting to be cut up and suffocated. This year, European and American countries have felt the dumping of Japanese goods, and twenty-seven countries have jointly worked to resist it by increasing taxes, restricting imports, issuing import permits, and managing exchange rates. Even Japan itself has measures to control import and export trade. The government and the industry stand on the same front, taking unified action. Their vision, flexibility, and policy sophistication, and the comprehensiveness of their prevention methods have been reported in various newspapers. Only our country, which has a large trade deficit, turns a blind eye and allows foreign goods to seize our market and suck our marrow, leading us to a point of no return. I know that anyone with blood and a conscience cannot bear to sit idly by. I would like to briefly state my opinions as follows:

(1) The National Economic Council should promptly prepare for the establishment of an Import and Export Trade Control Bureau to conduct thorough research on whether there are substitutes for the most foreign goods, and make every effort to restrict them.

(2) The Thick Production National Standard Mark Ordinance has already been promulgated. The government should implement it promptly, without further extensions, so as not to miss the opportunity to develop domestic products.

(3) Shanghai's various organizations and institutions should continue the spirit of this year in 1934 for the Second National Products Year, and mobilize for a while. It is best to use all our energy and strength to promote and use domestic products in this year.

(4) The government should issue a circular to all agencies and schools across the country that any foreign goods found in the procurement of goods will not be reimbursed.

(5) The government or local organizations should organize a National Products Committee to review or identify imported goods and study whether there are substitutes for them, so as to encourage imitation.

(6) It is said that 1934 will be officially designated as the Women's National Products Year. From now on, the general ladies, grandmothers, and young ladies will bear greater and more meaningful responsibilities. I sincerely hope that everyone will work hard.

(7) All schools across the country, large, medium, and small, should unite and work hard in this national products movement, carrying out a general mobilization of the national academic community.

(8) The national products promotion in 1934 should start from practical aspects. Rather than issuing empty arguments, it is better to show our true skills.

If the whole country can do this, the 900 million yuan trade deficit may be reduced year by year, and even eliminated. It depends on the strength of the government and the determination of the Chinese people.

National Products Talk

Don't Use Foreign Goods, Don't Get Married

— Natural

Mr. Zhang Fengshan of the Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center has organized a marriage reform association. Most of the local people have joined this association. However, the first condition for marriage reform is, "Don't use foreign goods, don't get married." It is said that the supervision is very strict, and the correction is very severe. If one of the new couple is a little careless and buys foreign goods, then without hesitation, they are asked to postpone the wedding. From head to toe, from top to bottom, every shoe, every sock, every thread, must be entirely domestic goods. Otherwise, no matter how affectionate you are, you are not allowed to become a beautiful couple, or complete a good marriage. This approach is a good example of promoting domestic goods. Extending this further, matchmakers can also put on a stern face and say: If you don't use domestic goods, I won't be a matchmaker. Wedding officiants can also sit upright and say, if you don't use domestic goods, I won't officiate your wedding. In this way, every pair of new couples will use domestic goods, and every little baby born next year will also use domestic goods. Then, if Chinese people use Chinese goods, even if there are many foreign goods, who will patronize them? The import surplus of 900 million yuan may gradually decrease, even to the point of disappearing.

Women and Domestic Goods

— Yingdai

Undoubtedly, in a family managed by a housewife who dislikes using foreign goods, it is difficult for foreign goods to gain a foothold. Therefore, a virtuous housewife should be a pioneer in promoting domestic goods. If her husband buys foreign goods, she should not only not welcome them but also rebuke him. This will make her husband not only afraid to buy foreign goods for his wife but also afraid to buy them for himself. As a result, in the family managed by this virtuous housewife, foreign goods will have no room to extend their reach.

However, how many such housewives are there in the big city of Shanghai where we live? To be honest, they are truly rare. Most housewives in Shanghai not only do not know that they have the mission of promoting domestic goods, but they always love to use foreign goods in the opposite direction. If they ask a man to buy something outside, if it is domestic goods, even if it is very good, they will say it is not good; if it is foreign goods, even if it is not good, it is good. As a result, every family is filled with traces of foreign goods. We cannot blame women entirely, but women are at least responsible for more than half of the problem.

The bad habit of women who love to use foreign goods is not formed overnight, but is cultivated from childhood by various influences from the environment. A young girl, born into a middle- or upper-class family, whose parents are the vanguard of loving to use foreign goods, so in her childhood, what she hears and sees early on is the idea that foreign goods are better than domestic goods. In school, most of the female classmates are the same, sharing the same ailment, and everyone worships foreign goods. In adolescence, the only important condition for making boyfriends is to be a young man who wears a Western suit. If someone's lover doesn't wear a Western suit but wears Chinese clothing, they are a bumpkin, and it is truly embarrassing! Once they become housewives, the psychology of loving to use foreign goods has already taken root and cannot be changed.

Under such circumstances, in their youth, most men remove their Chinese clothing and put on Western suits as the first important thing in order to cater to women's main conditions for making friends. Once they have a lover, they eat Western food, give foreign goods and imported goods as gifts. When the relationship matures and they get married, the wife worships foreign goods, so naturally, they use as much foreign goods as possible to enhance the feelings between husband and wife. Under these circumstances, countless foreign goods invade ordinary Chinese families, causing Chinese people to pay a lot of money to foreign countries every year!

Foreign goods are able to flood the Chinese market, and the Chinese people, both men and women, should bear the blame, but we feel that women are an even more important factor. If a housewife can promote domestic goods as much as possible and reject foreign goods, then the power of foreign goods in China will not be difficult to eliminate immediately. Therefore, a virtuous housewife should be a pioneer in promoting domestic goods. If all the housewives in China can take on the mission of promoting domestic goods, the result will definitely be the overthrow of foreign goods, making them disappear from the Chinese market!

Offering Opinions

The Service Spirit That Employees of Domestic Goods Businesses Should Have

— Quan Jia

I believe that to seek the development of domestic goods businesses, the most important thing to pay attention to is the service ethics of employees. To go one step further, this is the most effective advertisement. We should enthusiastically utilize it in our domestic goods businesses. Xiaozong Wu said it very well in "Life in Japan."

"...No matter how much effort you give him (referring to the merchant) in a Japanese store, no matter how you choose goods, if you can't find what you want, you can just not buy it. When you leave his store, he will still kneel down and salute you very respectfully, and say, 'Thank you, please come again next time!' He will never make you feel even a little unhappy."

The stone of another mountain can be used to polish jade. This is not the case with Chinese stores. If you don't buy anything and take up a lot of his time, the polite ones will give you a look of disdain, and the impolite ones will give you a condescending look or even scold you. This is the reason for the failure of Chinese businesses. In fact, you should ask yourself, why don't people like your goods? On the one hand, you can compare the goods and prices to see if they are worth buying. There is a Western proverb: "The buyer's eye is the fairest." If you often think about this, your business will not fail. Employees of our domestic goods businesses! We should seriously change our bad habits from the past. This is the most economical advertising technique!

We should not exaggerate the goodness of the goods, as this only exposes the Chinese people's ability to lie and refuses customers to visit a second time. We must sincerely explain to customers that domestic goods urgently need the support of the public. Even if they don't buy anything, we must be friendly.

The Chinese Vocational Education Society has obtained the conditions required by the industry for apprentices: honesty, responsibility, loyalty, trustworthiness, obedience, diligence, hard work, and health.

Strive! This is our business creed.
