Discussion of Domestic Goods

Cost Accounting System and Domestic Goods Business

— Zhou Chengxun

At present, the authorities of general domestic goods businesses, in addition to often thinking about expanding operations and improving products, there is another thing that can be said to be urgently planned and busily calculated, which is the issue of the cost of production. Indeed, if we find a manager or director of a domestic goods factory and ask him how much material is needed for a certain product? How much labor? What is the total cost? It can be said with certainty that there is no specific answer. They calculate periodically and settle accounts annually, only knowing how much surplus or deficit there is, but what is the fundamental cause of the surplus or deficit? Which products can make a profit? Which products are actually losing money? There is no way to show. Therefore, a cost accounting system is very worthy of being urgently adopted and implemented by business operators, especially in the fledgling domestic goods industry.

The general public mistakenly believes that the scope of cost only includes all raw material and labor costs in manufacturing. In fact, it is not that narrow. For every item sold, its cost, in addition to the above part, should also include the expenses of personnel management and sales promotion, and then the total cost can be obtained. In other words, it is not enough for a factory to obtain the cost of all products, because this is general and unclear. We must find out the unit cost of each product. These points in particular must rely on cost accounting.

Is the domestic goods business showing a vigorous vitality today? But if you only work on publicity and sales and ignore the cost, this step is unreasonable. Anyway, a factory can truly understand the unit cost of various products, and only then can it have reliable preparation for formulating sales prices and establishing profits in business policies. Moreover, in the recent bad situation of competition among the same industries, in order to establish one's own footing and resist external struggles, cost accounting is a truly powerful aid.

Checking many larger-scale domestic goods factories, it is rare to find those that implement a cost accounting system. In fact, to establish a cost accounting system, you must first have a sound accounting organization. Many authorities of domestic goods factories like to adhere to the old-fashioned accounting and are unwilling to reform and utilize it well. This is absolutely wrong. Now I dare to list several points below about the effectiveness of cost accounting for businesses:

(1) Because under the cost accounting system, all raw materials, semi-finished products, and finished products are recorded in detail, completely, accurately. Using the book inventory method, the quantity of storage, receipt, issue, and inventory can be displayed daily, thereby preventing the malpractices of waste, misuse, and leakage.

(2) Various products have separate cost calculations to distinguish the profits and losses of various products, which can provide operators with a policy for making choices in manufacturing.

(3) From the above results, a suitable and profitable selling price can be formulated for each product.

(4) The cost calculations of previous years can be collected, analyzed, and compared to report to investors. Moreover, because the source of profits in previous years is clearly indicated, it can be used as a reference for future operations.

(5) Under the cost accounting system, even if personnel are frequent and management is complex, because each department has clear levels of office and each has a chain of responsibility, an internal restraint organization is indirectly formed.

(6) All factories in the same industry have real cost calculations, which can be compared with each other to determine ways to save expenses and reduce costs.

Based on the above points, it is determined that the benefits that the cost accounting system gives to the business are very large. The authorities who operate domestic goods businesses should first recognize that cost accounting is the best aid for business progress and should never cherish the mental and financial resources when preparing for implementation. At the same time, the old-fashioned accounting, which largely lacks the cultivation of principles, should be abolished and new-style accounting should be implemented first, and then the cost accounting system can be discussed.

The main purpose of this article is to explain the close relationship between the cost accounting system and the domestic goods business. As for how to design and implement it, it is not within the scope of this article. I would like to leave it for further discussion!

Random Thoughts on Domestic Goods

— Qinian

To cultivate future citizens to use domestic goods, mothers must take more responsibility to instill the concept of loving domestic goods in children's minds.

To avoid the temptation of foreign goods, it is best to avoid living in Western-style houses, because the decoration of Western-style houses always requires foreign goods.

Hosts of banquets should be ashamed of using shark fins and other enemy goods. In fact, using those does not necessarily show your wealth, but rather shows your personality.

"Every thread and every grain of rice should remind you of how hard it was to obtain." should be changed to "Every thread and every object must be checked to see if its origin is domestic goods."

What shop assistants say is sometimes unreliable, so to buy domestic goods, it is best to go to honest and reliable domestic goods places.

You cannot completely blindly follow; you should also discern when others persuade you to buy something and you suspect it is foreign goods.

No matter where you can wield authority (such as in the family or in society), you should be a model of promoting domestic goods. This will naturally be more effective than having low-level people shout about promoting domestic goods. However, you must be consistent in your words and deeds to avoid losing their trust.

Most of the trademarks that use foreign words are cosmetics and cigarettes. They say they are taking advantage of the customer's psychology, but they are actually committing suicide in terms of their own sales.

At the end of the Domestic Goods Year, what we look forward to is only the impression of several domestic goods parades and domestic goods promotions. I would like to propose that domestic goods companies and stores form a "Domestic Goods Street," so that not only will it be convenient for customers to purchase, but the products will also compete to improve.

Random Talk on Domestic Goods

How to Protect Skin in Winter

— Ms. He Liying

▲ Night Cream among Domestic Goods

Winter is here, and in order to protect their delicate faces, young men and women in general have made cosmetics such as cold cream their only benefactor. Oh! "Snow" and "Frost" abound, with so many varieties that the eyes are dazzled, and the masses each choose and buy the items they love.

However, well-manufactured items such as cold cream can indeed form a thin film on the skin's surface, preventing the invasion of wind and sun, and at the same time, making the skin white, delicate, and maintaining its youthful beauty. It is especially necessary to use cold cream as a base before applying powder and rouge. However, if you use inferior products, there will be the disadvantage of blocking pores! Therefore, you must choose carefully when purchasing cold cream.

Cold creams can be roughly divided into two types: one is for daytime use, which is non-greasy cold cream (Western name: Day Cream). Most of the cold creams sold on the market are of this type. The other is for nighttime use before going to bed, which is greasy cold cream (Western name: Night Cream). This product has long become a daily cosmetic staple in European and American countries. Especially in winter, human skin naturally contracts due to the cold weather, feeling a lack of fat and dryness. Therefore, artificial fatty cold cream must be relied upon to moisturize it and promote the metabolism of the skin itself.

Now, this kind of night cream has also been produced in fine quality among domestic goods. As far as I know, the "Fangze Zhi" produced by the China Chemical Industry Society is a very beautiful fatty cold cream.

The color of Fangze Zhi is exceptionally lovely and pure white, and the fragrance has a subtle almond scent. When you put it on your arms, head, and neck before going to bed, the oily substance it contains can penetrate the pores, removing all the dirt and grease received during the day, directly making the skin white and radiant, and preventing roughness, chapping, frostbite, and other problems on the skin. It is indeed a benefactor for beauty-loving ladies during this winter season.

Finally, I have one more thing to tell readers, which is that the price of this product is half the price of similar foreign products, so it is also very economical.

A Domestic Goods Pilgrimage in the Countryside

— Xuan Wan

This time, because of illness, I took leave and returned to my hometown. In this huge, monster-like temple, I left the paper-drunk and gold-obsessed city and arrived at my already dilapidated village—a small town in western Zhejiang. Having not returned for more than a year, everything naturally seemed different to me. The once bustling market is now deserted and frightening. The successive failures of silk and rice are naturally their fatal wounds. Seeing the calloused hands and feet of the farmers, after several layers of deep and painful wounds, their faces, which were full of deep wrinkles, were filled with depression and lifelessness. "The countryside is bankrupt," this cry has already been heard numbly and witnessed with my own eyes. After I felt deep pain in this, I was filled with a burst of excitement due to natural arousal, and I went on a domestic goods pilgrimage in the countryside.

Sure enough, most of the items in the countryside are still purely local goods. However, as long as you inspect the few foreign goods and sundry stores in the market, you will be greatly surprised. Seven or eight out of ten of the items filling the store cabinets and windows are completely authentic foreign goods, and most of these foreign goods are enemy goods. They are completely using dumping tactics, leading to the lowest prices, to seduce our ignorant villagers, whose purchasing power is weak to the extreme. The malicious intentions and despicable measures are beyond indignation. As for the real countryside, on the banks of the fields and on the rice threshing floors, there are only a few shouting vendors, their clear throats carrying a pair of heavy loads, what with washbasins! Overshoes! Towels and socks! ... All the daily necessities of rural families can often be seen in our domestic goods here. However, they are all inferior goods, and even more inferior goods. This is probably due to price considerations!

Although relieving the countryside and resisting enemy goods are our entire problems, which cannot be solved in a short time, we are ultimately too dissatisfied with witnessing this strange phenomenon. The impression it gives us is that farmers' weak purchasing power leads to opportunistic activity of enemy goods and rampant merchants taking advantage of this. Therefore, we should now use direct advertising or effective publicity, preferably to reduce costs and sell at low prices, to first influence the villagers, and then gradually seek a thorough method of resistance. As for my review of domestic goods in the countryside this time, although it cannot represent the entire countryside, it at least gave us a very good lesson and aroused our attention later on.

Visit Notes

Notes on Visiting the National Exhibition of the Young Women's Christian Association

— Zhang Mengzhao

The words "Domestic Goods Year" will soon be quickly rotated away with the giant wheels of the era of 1933! As we examine the past and look to the future, we cannot help but feel sad! Feel heartbroken! What is sad is that patriots are shouting loudly, calling for the promotion of domestic goods and alerting compatriots, but: how many people can reform and be happy to use local goods? The facts tell us, it is simply heartbreaking to look back!

What is heartbreaking is that foreign goods are becoming more rampant with the domestic goods movement! Isn't it? Do the statistics on the import of grease incense powder, as the newspapers tell us, sound horrifying? As the new and old years are about to alternate, there are two domestic goods exhibitions, making a final struggle! Effort! One is the Shanghai Special District Domestic Goods Movement Conference sponsored by the China National Products Manufacturers Association, and the other is the Women's Domestic Goods Exhibition sponsored by the Shanghai Young Women's Christian Association, shining with great light at the end of this year! I believe that the latter is more urgent and more necessary than the former, because from the standpoint of Chinese women, they hold full power over the rise and fall of domestic goods. The diet, clothing, and household utensils of husbands, sons, and daughters all depend on the lady of the house. Therefore, on the opening day of the association's domestic goods exhibition, I eagerly drove to see it with Yunqing, to learn from it. Although this very meaningful grand event of the National Exhibition was held in the imperialist concession of the ten-mile foreign market and in tall Western-style buildings, it gave us Chinese a very deep and far-reaching impression! After our visit, we were very satisfied! The satisfying thing is that the display of domestic goods does not emphasize stiffness but emphasizes three-dimensional and active styles. The most valuable thing here is the "Model Family" arranged by the China National Products Company! The domestic goods displayed, such as steel beds, dressing tables, wardrobes, drawers, rattan chairs, and mahogany furniture, are actually bright and clean, shining in the eyes. They are divided into three grades: 500 yuan, 1,000 yuan, and 2,000 yuan. It is truly a good program for people to emulate. The 2,000-yuan family seems too aristocratic. Those who are capable can of course follow suit, but ordinary people should still follow the 500-yuan style! On that day, the young men and women who visited the model family, as far as we could see, all had a very deep interest, and they would definitely have a very deep impression when they returned, and everyone would be happy to use domestic goods! I mean, don't open a domestic goods exhibition in the future! If you want to open one, you should take the three-dimensional and active styles. In other words, you must conduct on-site tests. For example, if the Sanyou Society's free cloth wants to show that it does not fade, it should be hung in the center of the water for everyone to see. The national cloth umbrella should be propped up under the sprinklers, showing its tightness and practicality. This is the most important point.

Secondly, the good impression we had after the visit was that in the speech contest for elementary school students, "The Responsibility of Students to Promote Domestic Goods," even the small minds had a recognition of domestic goods. Jin Jiaomei, a female student from Qingxin School, was very young, but she was able to give a passionate and generous speech on the stage, how to use domestic goods, how to overthrow foreign goods, and save the country. Her eloquence was so good that even adults were ashamed. Such a thought of loving domestic goods, deeply imprinted in the minds of the young masters, will surely be able to recover the lost rights and interests, and domestic goods will always have a way out. I wonder how the modernized grandmothers and wives felt after hearing her speech and blushing?

Children's World

Bright Son and Domestic Goods

— Smoke Shadow

Bright Son is thirteen years old this year, studying in elementary school. He listened to his teachers and parents, knows very well to love the country, and loves to use domestic goods very much. We can take a look at the letters he wrote:

(I)

Brother Zhicheng:

I received your letter yesterday and was very happy. You even sent me two kinds of toys, I am truly grateful!

However, although these two toys are very good and I also love to play with them, I don't think they are domestic goods. I heard people say that there are many people buying these things on the streets recently, they are all foreign goods. I don't know where you bought yours?

Now our domestic goods also have this kind of toy, which is made even more interesting and sturdy than foreign goods. My father once bought one for me to play with. I think we are Chinese citizens and should use Chinese domestic goods, so I don't want what you sent.

I am returning what you sent, and sending you two domestic toys instead. You also heard what my teacher said, we must never buy foreign goods. Please buy more domestic goods in the future, and don't blame me!

School is about to start, how happy! Goodbye! Wishing you

Good health! Brother Bright Son

(II)

Dear Older Sister:

It has been several months since we parted. We all miss you very much. How is your health?

Yesterday, Second Cousin came to our house. He bought a lot of clothing material, saying that you asked him to buy it. I saw that this kind of clothing material is all foreign goods, and the price is very expensive, several dollars a foot. Alas! I am extremely sad!

Dad often says: "China's poverty and weakness are all because the people don't love the country. Everyone likes to buy foreign goods and give money to foreigners, so our industry is delayed from developing." Haven't you heard what Dad said? You also agreed with it very much, you used to tell me to love the country too, why are you buying foreign goods now?

Not to mention other things, silk is originally a product of our country, and has recently been improved even more. It is said that it is not inferior to foreign goods, but the price is much cheaper. Then we should naturally buy domestic silk to make clothes, don't you think so?

The reason I am writing this letter is to advise you to buy domestic goods for everything in the future. Goodbye! Wishing you

Patriotism! Younger Brother Bright Son

(III)

Dear Second Cousin:

We were very happy when you came to our house the day before yesterday, but it's a pity that you went back so soon.

I admire what you said about buying foreign goods. Alas! Why do our compatriots all like to buy foreign goods? It's really regrettable! You said that the things used in various institutions are almost all foreign goods, is this true? I don't believe it, don't they know how to love the country? Our teacher said that the government is now vigorously promoting domestic goods, but you say that they use a lot of foreign goods, what is the reason for this?

I think there is another kind of people who also buy a lot of foreign goods, and that is women. Look at the clothing material my older sister asked you to buy, the price is expensive, and it's not like there is no domestic silk that can be used to make clothes. Their powder, perfume, all have to be foreign goods, alas! They really have no conscience!

You said that only we elementary school students love the country the most, but we dare not accept that compliment. We just all want to be good citizens, and hope that our four hundred million compatriots will all be of one mind to love the country, and all buy domestic goods with one heart, that would be great! Wishing you

Good health! Cousin Bright Son

Short Story

The Wedding Night

— Cold Jade

It was already four o'clock, and the guests who made merry in the bridal chamber had all left. However, everything in the room had a lively atmosphere. After the excitement and noise, the bride and groom were no longer tired. So, the groom suddenly asked:

"Jingyi: I have a question to ask you." The bride was startled and glanced at the groom. The groom continued: "Among the things you bought this time, which country's goods are the most?"

The bride's heart instantly relaxed. After a pause, she replied: "You can rest assured about that. The things I bought this time are all domestic goods."

"Whose idea was it?"

The bride slowly replied: "After the September 18th Incident, I joined the Domestic Goods Ten-Person Group..."

"You also joined the Domestic Goods Ten-Person Group?" The groom asked hastily, "Then we are truly comrades."

The bride continued: "The reason I joined is because I saw that the best way for our people to save the country is to use domestic goods. Only through economic resistance can we truly make the country prosper. Moreover, women in the city should be role models for women across the country, but now they are all using foreign goods. Can this be a role model for the whole country? So I resolutely decided to use domestic goods. After using them, I know that the quality of domestic goods is not worse than that of foreign goods, so why use foreign goods? This is truly a shame for us urban women."

The groom casually picked up a few things on the table to look at, and they were all printed with the trademarks of domestic goods. He was extremely happy and said to the bride: "You are truly the wife of my dreams. Let's make another oath today, we will never use foreign goods."

"We will never use foreign goods."

Spring and Autumn

Re-election in the Realm of Poetry

— Smoke Bridge

The poet Mr. Jin Hewang, in previous years, had a playful work on the election of the realm of poetry. At that time, it was still the era of the president, so the characters he chose were:

President: Gu Yanwu Vice President: Qu Dajun

Prime Minister: Zeng Guofan Minister of Interior: Fan Dangshi

Minister of Foreign Affairs: Huang Zunxian Minister of Finance: Fan Zengxiang

Minister of Education: Wang Shizhen Minister of Justice: Shen Deqian

Minister of Transportation: Yuan Mei Minister of Industry: Cheng Jinfang

Minister of the Army: Zhao Wenzhe Minister of the Navy: Qiu Canghai

Of the poets mentioned above, apart from Gu, Qu, Zeng, Huang, Fan, Wang, Shen, and Yuan, everyone knows their life stories. For example, Fan Dangshi, also known as Kentang, was from Tongzhou. His poetry combined the strengths of Su and Huang, and he had a collection of Fan Bozi. Cheng Jinfang, also known as Yumen, with the pen name Jieyuan, was from Shexian, and had the Jieyuan Poetry Collection. Zhao Wenzhe, with the style name Sunzhi, and the pen name Puhan, was from Shanghai, and had the Yatang Collection. During the Qianlong era, he followed Minister Wenfu to quell the Jinchuan rebellion, and died in battle, he was a scholarly warrior. Qiu Canghai was from Taiwan, and died more than ten years ago. The criteria for the election were not only based on their poetry, but also on their scholarship and conduct. Yuan Zicai traveled widely, and was indeed suitable for transportation. Shen Guiyu had a dignified appearance, which was in line with the Ministry of Justice. It can be considered that his reputation matched his position, and he was not unworthy of his duties.

As time passes, talents naturally need to be replaced. Therefore, Mr. Hewang published an announcement in the second issue of the Guoxue Lunheng, published by the Guoxue Society, asking the members to re-elect. The results will be published in the third issue. Those who cling to the past and die in obscurity can breathe a sigh of relief in the netherworld. Moreover, this kind of election is very fair. Those who are alive have no right to be elected. Poetry ghosts will not be able to campaign. Even if there is a wisp of a poetic soul to guide the pen, the electors can still act with integrity and not cater to anyone's preferences.

This kind of game has been around for a long time among literati. For example, Lu Juren's Jiangxi School Chart was the originator. In the mid-Qing Dynasty, Shu Wei had the Qianlong Jia Poetry Scene Commanders' Record, which compared poets to heroes of Liangshan Marsh. Although the comparison was not perfect, it was still stubborn and pleasing. It is a pity that there were too many positions, which inevitably led to excessiveness. In my opinion, it is necessary to conform to the modern system, and below the chairman, set up departments and divisions, so that the origins and schools can be more easily traced.

Edward Road More Than Twenty Years Ago

— Zheng Yimei

The situation in Shanghai is truly changing every five years and transforming drastically every decade. No matter how old you are in Shanghai, as long as you leave for a few years, you will be somewhat dazed and confused, unable to recognize which is Nanjing Road and which is Fuzhou Road. All you see are towering buildings, magnificent mansions, and neon lights everywhere, a scene of prosperity that stirs the heart and mind. I once heard my late grandfather, Mr. Jinting, talk about when he first arrived in Shanghai, the area north of Nanjing Road was completely barren, full of graves and cemeteries. Fujian Road was still a river, with wild boats moored randomly, full of rural scenery. Today, it has transformed into a bustling urban area with dense population and endless traffic. It was definitely beyond his wildest dreams back then.

I was born late, so of course I didn't see the earliest Shanghai. However, I still remember the situation of Edward Road more than twenty years ago. At that time, my late grandfather was still alive and well. We had properties in both Shanghai and Suzhou. I lived in Shanghai and studied at the Duren School along the city wall. Every day on my way to school, I had to pass through Edward Road. At that time, Edward Road was a foreign creek, serving as the natural boundary between the British and French concessions. Bridges were built over the creek for people to pass back and forth, which is why there are still names like Dai Gou Bridge, Zhengjia Wooden Bridge, and Dongxin Bridge to this day. The north bank of the creek was the British concession, and the embankment was built relatively well. However, the south bank of the creek, which was the French concession, was dilapidated and overgrown with weeds. Crabs grew in the gaps in the mud on the embankment. Every day after school, I often climbed onto the dilapidated embankment with a few mischievous classmates to catch crabs. Although the crabs were small, their claws were very sharp. If we weren't careful, we would bleed our fingers. However, due to our naughty nature, we didn't care about the pain and caught as many as we could, putting them in the largest cigarette box, which was completely filled. We also used a tin biscuit box, accumulating wet clay inside, digging holes so that the crabs could enter and exit, and giving them some food. In this way, the crabs' lives were extended for a few days. The childhood scene is still vivid in my memory, just like yesterday. Now, Edward Road has become the widest thoroughfare in all of Shanghai, with high buildings on both sides and densely packed shops. When it's time for office workers to go to and from work, the motorcycles speed by like lightning, one after another. The traces of the old days are nowhere to be found. If I were to talk about catching crabs there now, wouldn't it become a joke?

Lamenting General Autumn

— Lean Qing

Crickets, small autumn insects, and people like to pit them against each other in fights, competing for victory, and even spending thousands of dollars without hesitation. Then, these people naturally value crickets almost more than the outstanding heroes and strongmen among humans. The other night, the local police cracked down on a cricket fighting venue, and more than seventy famous people were arrested and taken to the police station. Apart from those who were released on bail for several hundred dollars at the time, the others are still being held. Later, they were taken to the Special District Local Court, where fines were imposed with varying amounts. The cricket breeders, although fined, don't consider it a big deal. However, many "Generals" (people here call crickets by this title) were trampled on by them at the time, their pots and jars were broken, their heads and feet were incomplete, and they died suddenly on the spot. This is truly the most regrettable and hateful thing. A friend sent me a "funeral notice" the other day. I couldn't help but laugh when I saw it. This "funeral notice" was actually for a cricket's funeral. So, the "funeral notice" said:

Condolences, General Bai Qingqiu, passed away in our bedroom due to illness at the hour of Wei (1-3 PM) on November 22nd of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, having been acquired on the Shen (3-5 PM) of the third day before the Mid-Autumn Festival of the lunar calendar, at the age of fifty days. A grave will be dug on December 20th and buried in the western part of our garden, with an inscription that reads "The Tomb of General Bai Qingqiu." Those who have an affinity for autumn, please accept this announcement!

This friend can be considered extremely humorous. He also attached a personal letter, explaining: "This General was bought from Hangzhou for 340 silver dollars at the time. He has fought three times and can be called an invincible, ever-victorious General. Unexpectedly, he suffered this misfortune this time. Although he was not guilty of fighting and was able to return from danger, he has been experiencing constant changes in temperature in recent days, and his care was inadequate. When I looked at him this morning, he was already stiff. Alas, alas!" After reading the words in the letter, I couldn't help but laugh, but I also had to write a few words of mourning and follow the usual social customs to respond to my friend. So I picked up my pen and wrote a lament to mourn him, and sent it to my friend:

Alas, you little autumn insect, why couldn't you rest quietly? Your chattering chirping annoyed the playful children. In the end, amidst the broken walls and broken houses, you destroyed your home. You couldn't lie low and leisurely, and instead entered the cage. Elegant people named it Autumn Interest, and all claimed to be followers of Jia Sidao. Who would have thought that your white teeth and green scales (i.e., the General's special features) and your coir raincoat, golden belt, moon forehead, and delicate features (other Generals' advantages) were irrelevant. In defeat, you would collapse and retreat in a panic, but in victory, you would plant a red flag and turn it red in an instant. However, at the time of engagement, you had no autonomy, and were entirely at the mercy of people's instigation and manipulation. Alas, so much gold was spent on your one beak, and your loyalty was in vain, and people's pockets were emptied. What's more, it was like gambling and arresting generals in the official's quarters, which is not allowed by law, and fines were imposed. This is no different from today's warlords who willingly become leaders of the army. Although they occupy territory and call themselves heroes, they ultimately become a laughingstock and sacrifice themselves in vain. Why bother to unleash your power and recklessly do something beyond your ability? I mourn the General's flapping wings and bared fangs, and his misfortune. I have no choice but to offer these words to awaken those who are dreaming.

Talking About Year-End Reports

— New

Every year during the New Year in the solar or lunar calendar, because major newspapers suspend publication, people who seek to make a quick buck by publishing year-end reports emerge, hoping to earn some extra income. Three years ago, major newspapers suspended publication for as many as nine days, which was indeed a large influx of money, so there were as many as twenty or more kinds of year-end reports. Their sales ranged from hundreds to thousands of copies. However, the fewer the sales, the more income they received. The amount of advertising they pulled in depended on their individual efforts, which was their income. Now, in order to compete, major newspapers suspend publication for three days from New Year's Day, but during these three days, they issue extra editions, accept all advertising, and notify all movie theaters and shops in advance. As a result, the year-end reports of those who seek to make a quick buck are like a bolt from the blue, receiving a death sentence. Therefore, there are not a few who cancel their plans temporarily. This can be considered their most disappointing thing.

Northeast Four Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 20: Predicting Good Fortune, the Old Man Smiles Daily; Dispelling Endless Worries, Old Friends Live Across the Street

When Guizhi turned her head, it was Aunt Liu, the newly arrived maid of the Gan family. She didn't know about Guizhi's past dealings with the Gan family, so she replied: "She's been lying at home these past few days. She only got a little better today." Aunt Liu said: "Isn't that right? Now there's another seasonal illness. Our master is very ill, and all the relatives in the city have come to see him." Guizhi asked: "What kind of illness is it that's so serious? Has your Second Master come too?" Aunt Liu said: "He's been here for several days. He's been taking care of most of the patient's affairs. He also asked me about it..." Saying this, she glanced at Guizhi and smiled slightly. Guizhi pretended not to care and casually asked: "What did he ask about?" Aunt Liu smiled: "He asked when you were getting married. He said he has a very good relationship with your company commander and is prepared to give a generous gift." Guizhi blushed and smiled: "I think you're making that up. Why would he ask about my whereabouts?" Aunt Liu said: "I'm really telling the truth. You'll understand when you meet him another day." Guizhi felt an infinite amount of emotion when she heard these words. She stood there stunned, holding the small package in her hand. Aunt Liu didn't want to say more to her and turned around to leave. Guizhi stood there for a while. When she looked up, Aunt Liu had already walked away. She thought that it would be boring to just stand there, so she took the package and went to Wang the tailor's house. About an hour later, she walked back to the original place. When she reached the entrance of the Gan family, she stretched her head and looked into their courtyard to see if there was anything else going on. Just as she was looking, Gan Jizhi was walking from east to west in the courtyard. He didn't expect anyone to be peeking at him outside the gate, so he looked ahead and didn't see Guizhi. However, Guizhi's heart skipped a beat, and she couldn't help but shrink back. By the time Jizhi had walked past, she pretended to have lost something and kept pacing around in the alley, but constantly stealing glances inside the gate. After pacing for a long time, Jizhi was finally unable to come out again, so she had no choice but to lower her head and slowly walk home. (273)

Small Gardening

Shanghai Flower Shops

— Chen Bijun

Flowers can cultivate temperament, flowers can delight the mood. We often like to stop and gaze when passing by flower shops, appreciating them. The magic of flowers is indeed not small. In recent years, new methods of cultivation have become popular, and the cultivation of flowers has been promoted. Flower shops are opening up more and more, which is also a kind of emerging industry.

In Shanghai, flower shops are mostly concentrated in the areas of Sichuan Road, Xiejiao General Assembly, and Avenue Joffre. Under the bright glass windows, there are exquisitely crafted flower baskets, and around them are red, green, and five-colored flowers and leaves. Occasionally stepping inside is like being in a fragrant kingdom, surrounded by green and red. It is said that the arrangement of flower shop windows is best in the western district. Affluent families also attach neon lights to the glass windows. When the night market arrives, the lights are bright and illuminating, enveloping the delicate flower branches, making them look even more energetic. The skills of making flower baskets are unmatched in the old Qichang area of Sichuan Road. Its products have uniform colors, are well-spaced, and have artistic ideas. In the last flower arrangement competition, a shop there won the first prize.

There is a flower market in the Nanyang Bridge area of Ximen. At dawn, various flowers gather in one place, with all kinds of colors and shapes. Flower shop owners all go there to purchase. Some flower shop owners cultivate flowers on their own land in the suburbs and sell their own products. In short, the flowers in the market are piled up like mountains, at everyone's disposal, and are not worthy of cherishing. Once they arrive at the flower shop, they are cherished, like a country girl who has entered the city, lightly touching up her eyebrows and wearing silk and satin, immediately becoming ten times more valuable. High-quality flowers are calculated by the bloom or bunch. The value of selling flower baskets and wreaths is at least two yuan each, and more can cost tens or even hundreds of yuan. Chinese people often like mixed colors, while Westerners prefer simplicity.

Flower shops opened by Chinese people mostly sell loose fresh flowers, with elaborate flower baskets and wreaths as the main business. Occasionally, they also arrange halls and wrap colored plaques for people. Japanese flower shops also sell bonsai rockeries and goldfish and birds, etc. Their store names seem to be more elegant, unlike ours, which are specially named with words such as "getting rich" and "smooth sailing." After looking at more than a hundred flower shops run by Chinese people, the signboards of Luchun in Xiejiao and Huandie Flower Shop in Guibal Road are among the best.

The improvement of customs cannot be regarded as the evolution of the city. The old陋习 of the past are gradually being eliminated now. Wreaths are sent for condolences, and flower baskets are used for weddings, birthdays, send-offs, and捧角. Even when visiting patients, a bunch of fresh flowers is sent to give them some sweet comfort in their painful environment. I remember when the League of Nations Manchuria Investigation Team passed through Tokyo, beautiful women sent flowers. This probably carried some媚意 in addition to respect.

The most prosperous seasons for flowers are late spring and summer, and the prices are also the cheapest. But康耐馨 are available in all seasons. Its colors are divided into three types: bright red, pink, and light white. Westerners love it the most, and they don't hesitate to spend one dollar to buy twelve blooms when it's expensive. Now that chrysanthemums have withered, flower shops still rely on it to struggle. The rest, yellow, white, and red monthly roses, and some ivory red, and year-round green mountain grasses, are lined up colorfully. The most fashionable are narcissus and white茨菇 flowers. Gladiolus and dahlias are inherently fertile. Dahlias have now disappeared, and gladiolus bloom in spring and summer. Recently, our country has often used to delay its planting period and extend it, so that it can be sold for a long time. It is a bulb, shaped like a chestnut, and its color is very diverse, the most common being light yellow. It has a thin membrane on the outside and has considerable resistance to the harsh winter. All year round, there are mostly洋花, and only 30% of flowers are本土.

I love to insert some fresh flowers in my desk and my bedroom. When the long night is漫漫 and the atmosphere is lonely, under the quiet lamplight or in the oblique moonlight, facing the flower color and feeling the flower fragrance, the漂泊人生 will get infinite comfort. It's a pity that after some time, the petals withered and the leaves withered. It was ignored by people and finally abandoned. Alas! The beauty of the past only leaves some melancholy in my heart, but the dreams of the young people have disappeared with the passing of time, and what is left is nothing more than some scars that are not easy to磨损.

However, the Fuzhou group originally had a strong appetite, but now that market prices have fallen flat, they are taking advantage of the small purchases and packing. The whole city sold 95 bags of unpolished rice from Fuzhou, 432 bags of unpolished rice from Shashi, 197 bags of unpolished rice from Nanjing, and 197 bags of Liu Xian rice. The Ningbo group only handled 100 bags of Yuan rice from Wuhu. The local shops handled 91 bags of Yuan rice from Jiangxi and 320 bags of Jing rice from Hunan. Currently, the market has no good prospects considering the sufficient supply and inventory. If sales to the southern provinces become stronger again and local hoarders continue to handle the rice, there may be a chance for a turnaround.

Peanuts Sell Well, Peanut Kernels Don't Move

Peanuts: Since their launch, their market has undergone changes, but sales in various locations have been continuous. Prices are more stable than peanut kernels. Yesterday, more than 1,000 bags of Tancheng goods were opened, with prices ranging from 4.9 yuan to 4.7 yuan. Apart from the Ningbo group taking 50 bags, the rest were handled by the local shops.

Peanut Kernels: The market is still not active. Exports are not moving, and factories and local shops are asking for information. No quotations were made yesterday. Although the source is small, there are approximately 50,000 to 60,000 bags of inventory. If there were more than 200,000 bags of inventory at this time in previous years, sentiment would still be flat. However, in this sluggish situation, there are 20,000 to 30,000 bags of inventory, so sentiment is nervous.

Southern and Northern Goods: New Large-Grained Longans Have Already Been Opened

The new large-grained longans from the second and third batches have not been opened for a long time because the cost is high and they do not fit the sales appetite. Now that goods are gradually becoming scarce and no new goods are continuing to arrive, the sellers' intentions are slightly active. Yesterday, it was heard that the shops had already sold one to two hundred boxes, with prices lower than the highest price by seven to eight yuan each. Although they are losing money, the sales channel is still small, and it is feared that the market will be difficult to recover.

Business Experience (50)

Various Kinds of Foreign Locks

Locks are needed for doors and equipment, and with the progress of machinery, Chinese-made locks are even considered to have simple structures and are almost extinct in urban areas. Locks shipped from the UK, US, Japan, and Germany, regardless of quality, have surprisingly gained a large sales volume, and these are commonly referred to as foreign locks.

The buying and selling of locks is calculated according to "gross" (one gross is ten dozen). The locks that are popular on the market are (1) square locks, which are commonly used, with the 808 and 710 models being the most common, and each model has different sizes; (2) insert locks, where the lock ball portion is matched with metal and enamel silver metal; (3) spring door locks, commonly known as spring locks, which have many distinctions, and the numbers are 3517, 2300, 2100, 2400, 2500, 4204, 4207, 1504, 6066, 111, 7140, etc.; (4) round locks, which come in sizes 16, 18, 19, and 21; (5) crescent locks, which are shaped like a crescent moon and come in six types, 15, 25, 35, 45, 55, and 65, and are distinguished by the size of the case; (6) white-covered locks, named because the lock body is covered with bright white metal, and the size is indicated by millimeter numbers on the lock body, such as 15, 25, 35, 45, 55, 65, and other sizes; (7) black locks and cupronickel-covered locks, with black and cupronickel coverings on the lock body, similar to spring and white-covered locks; (8) silver-plated locks, named because they are plated with silver, with sizes of 25, 35, 45, and 55; (9) brass locks, made of brass, with sizes of 25, 35, 45, and 55; (10) triangular locks, which are triangular, double-opening locks that can be opened on both sides, color locks, with various colors in the middle of the lock body, white lead locks, which are white lead gray, etc. Other lever-type, cylinder-type, and compass-type locks, with added triggers and hands, can be selected by those who need them.

Sugar Market: Xin Chao Qing Falls Another 4 Jiao

Yesterday the sugar market trend was relatively stable, and transactions were more active. The guild set the price for 24 coarse granulated white common goods at 19.75 yuan, down by 0.02, and about 600 bags were traded. Transshipment of Zi Jiao goods was 6.9 yuan, but the original price was not reached. The price of 20 medium granulated white common goods was 19.35 yuan, and the price of 89 grade He Chi SR goods was 15.8 yuan. The price of transshipped high-quality goods was 7.05 yuan. The price of Taikoo Sugar B mark was 20.25 yuan, unchanged, and the CW mark was down 0.02 to 20.008 yuan. The price of Xin Chao Qing brand fell another 0.4 jiao, and more than 300 bags were opened, with the price of Ti Zhuang Qing being 14 yuan, followed by 13.8 yuan to 13.5 yuan. The price of Zhen Ji Mian Bai No. 1 was 18.9 yuan, but no transactions were made.

Silk and Tea: No Sales Inside or Outside the Silk Market

▲Zhejiang Silk Industry Accumulates Cocoons, Difficult to Sell

Although there are more than twenty silk filatures in Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Huzhou, and Jiaxing in Zhejiang Province, only about four out of ten have managed to start work this autumn. Currently, only two or three are rushing to reel the remaining cocoons in preparation for closing down. However, the various manufacturers have a total of 15,000 piculs of unsold dry cocoons from the spring and autumn seasons, which can supply silk filatures with 2,700 to 2,800 piculs of silk. Among them, the Model Silk Filature and others have the largest stockpiles of cocoons. Sichuan and Hubei coarse silks are not selling well, with thick stocks in Shanghai and few new sources. A few days ago, the Jiangshun and other ships brought 38 pieces of Mianzhou and Mianyang yellow coarse silk, which were distributed to the Chunbao, Taihe, and other silk firms. As for the overseas market, Japanese silk prices have depreciated, and sales efforts are increasing. The various silk weaving factories cannot afford Chinese silk due to its high price. European and American silk sales still show no signs of improvement. The domestic silk shops also have no desire to purchase, as the end of the year is approaching. The market atmosphere is stagnant, and there is little market activity to report.

Imports of Artificial Silk Decrease Year by Year

丨Recent Transactions Also Sluggish丨

In recent years, the sales of artificial silk have replaced natural silk, resulting in annual imports consistently exceeding 10 million taels. According to customs reports, import statistics for the last four years show a gradual decrease. The reasons are the daily decline in the price of raw silk and the increase in import tariffs on artificial silk. Among the importing countries, Italy ranks first, followed by Germany and Japan. In 1930, the total imports were 127,091 piculs, with a value of 15,279,857 taels. In 1931, the imports were 123,349 piculs, with a value of 19,059,675 taels. In 1932, the imports were 103,388 piculs, with a value of 11,404,630 taels. From January to June of this year, the imports were 46,234 piculs, with a value of 4,289,878 taels. Recently, as the end of the year approaches, the demand for artificial silk has further decreased. Yesterday, only Meiya and other factories imported 20 cases of Golden Unicorn and Black Beauty brands, priced at 179.75 yuan net per package.

Free Talk

On Grand Funerals

— Yao Ke

The paraphernalia of grand funerals in China varies slightly from place to place; for example, the South has "path-opening gods," while the North has "snow willows"; but they are all pleasing to the eye and lively.

The most interesting thing about grand funerals is the tripartite system of Confucianism, Buddhism, and Taoism. The spirit tablet in the soul cart is a symbol of Confucianism; the monks and Taoists interspersed in the procession represent the authority of Buddhism and Taoism. The Chinese are thoroughly clever, incorporating all three teachings; the soul of the deceased either becomes a saint, a Buddha, or an immortal, like playing a thirty-six-door lottery, where at least one door will hit.

Foreigners, on the other hand, are foolish. They all worship the same God, but they insist on dividing into Catholicism, Christianity, Islam, Judaism, and other sects. The followers of each sect are as incompatible as birds' eyes and chickens, not understanding harmony, incorporation, or the wonderful method of playing a thirty-six-door lottery. Therefore, the souls of foreigners face the danger of making a single, all-or-nothing bet; if they miss, they will fall into the eighteenth level of Avici Hell, never to be redeemed.

The porters carrying flags and umbrellas in grand funerals are also intriguing. They are what Shanghainese call "despicable fellows," usually disheveled and dirty; the clothes they wear are not only dirty enough to "disgrace the nation," but also tattered enough to "offend public morals." But during grand funerals, they wear red-tasseled hats and embroidered robes, dignified and imposing, although their feet are still muddy under the robes.

The most important thing in a grand funeral seems to be the deceased in the coffin. The preciousness of the coffin and the extravagance of the burial goods are self-evident; just the pomp of the dragon-lai phoenix-tail crane-top, with its sixty-four bearers, is enough to see. But although the deceased in the coffin gets all the attention, it is actually just a front; the filial sons who have "extended the calamity to their late father" in the memorial announcements are the main characters of the grand funeral. The burly bodyguards only protect the filial sons, not the deceased, and the entire procession is just to enhance the prestige of the filial sons, not for the sake of the deceased's dignity!

Although the filial sons say "in mourning attire, confused and dazed," and "weeping blood and kowtowing" in the obituary, in fact, they are not confused at all during the grand funeral, and there may not be any real tears. The filial sons who owe a "mourning robe debt" are undoubtedly overjoyed in the memorial announcements. Even those who do not owe a mourning robe debt are preoccupied with the important matter of hiring lawyers to fight over the inheritance, so how could they keep the "late father's" will in mind? Even if the inheritance has already been divided and settled, they still need to plan to build new Western-style buildings and marry concubines...

The filial sons enjoy the inheritance, and it is indeed unspeakably delightful; the family's accountants, bodyguards, servants, and even the general attendants, monks, Taoists, drummers, bands, idlers, and the "despicable fellows" carrying flags and umbrellas also get some kickbacks, and everyone is happy.

As for the people watching the funeral procession, although they feast their eyes, they inevitably suffer some hardships. Losing shoes and hats and having their bags snatched are minor matters; if, unfortunately, there is a tragedy such as pregnant women being trampled or children getting lost, they can only "swallow their knocked-out teeth into their stomachs."

Some say: it would be best if there were no idle people watching the funeral procession, so that there would be no tragedies. That is true, but if no one is watching, there would be no grand funeral.

Meat and the Whip

— Ma Guoliang

When watching the performance of the Haijingbo Circus, I seemed to have a somewhat inexplicable feeling. Recently, I inadvertently saw the scene of them training wild animals in a movie, and I suddenly understood. Now I will roughly record it.

The curtain opens: the words "Animals in School" are written, and the words "Haijingbo's Method of Training Animals" are written.

F. I. Haijingbo stands outside the tiger cage and says a lot to the audience. Some of the words were unclear, and some were unclear. However, the general idea is nothing more than saying that training wild animals requires a lot of hard work and patience, etc. Then he began to show the training methods...

Watching a play is not like listening to words (and foreign words), so I saw it very clearly. But my memory is just as bad, and in many places, although I saw it clearly, I also made the mistake of not remembering clearly. But one thing that I will never forget now or in the future is: the trainer never lets go of the piece of meat and the whip!

The white-clad female trainer puts a piece of meat on a stool. There is another stool more than ten feet away from this stool, with a tiger standing on it. Then the female technician took a large ring between the two stools, on the one hand letting the tiger see the piece of meat, and on the other hand, the whip was shaking, so the tiger, which the world calls male and fierce, also lowered its ears and jumped through the ring, leaping to a stool on the opposite side and grabbing the piece of meat into its mouth. This is the training method for tigers to jump through rings.

Another set, tying the meat with a string, like fishing towards the dog's mouth. Holding the meat in the left hand and the whip in the right hand, the dog stands up like a human and can even dance.

Another set of cats climbing ladders, bears riding bicycles... Naturally, the meat bait and the whip are always together. Although some places are not shown on the movie screen, from the beginning to the success of the training, would you say that he did not use these two magic weapons?

After the piece of meat comes the whip, and after the whip comes the piece of meat, and there is a gentle embrace, so the tiger also piles up the Arhats, the monkey can also dance, and the fox can also practice boxing!

A gentleman sitting behind me couldn't help but marvel at his companion, saying that Haijingbo's methods were brilliant, but also lamented the weakness of the tiger.

I don't know why, but I think this person is really stupid. I wanted to tell him that what Haijingbo used was not some amazing smart method. This is just an old method. From a long time ago until now, many people have been using it, and it is as effective as Haijingbo's. I also wanted to tell him to hurry home and take a look in the mirror to see if he looked a bit like the face of that tiger or the head of that dog.

Of course, this was just a thought in my heart and I didn't really say it to him. I was afraid that when he asked me to look in the mirror too, I really wouldn't have the courage to take a mirror!

Suddenly, I thought of "Island of Lost Souls" again. I thought of the group of beasts who had been tortured and made into human form, and used as slaves, and finally realized that their master would die just like them, and finally killed their tyrant in the roar of "no more commandments." I couldn't help but worry a little for Haijingbo and his subordinates.

What if those tigers, leopards, lions, etc., also one day knew that their strength was greater than a whip, and knew that they would get more adequate food after destroying the whip?

Haijingbo has left Shanghai. I also have no intention of sending a telegram to warn him. Besides, do you think he would believe my words?

I feel that I am just as stupid as that person who was marveling!

Nalan Chengde's Poetics (Continued)

— Chen Ye

Four

Nalan Chengde's basic understanding of poetry is like this. Starting from this basis, he wrote poems and filled in lyrics, and studied ancient poetry, so he often had many insightful discussions. In "Lushuiting Miscellaneous Records," he criticized many ancient lyricists, such as Mei Cheng, Ruan Ji, Yu Zishan, Tao Yuanming, Xie Tiao, Changli, Wang Jian, Liu Yuxi, Dongpo, Shangu, Ouyang Xiu, Xin Qiji, Yuan Yishan, Zhao Wenmin, Yang Tieya, Yuan Yishan, and even Li Houzhu. In his criticism of these people, he had many good opinions. Many people call Nalan Chengde the reincarnation of Li Houzhu, so first let me introduce his "On Li Houzhu":

The lyrics of the Flower Collection are like ancient jade artifacts, precious but not practical. Song lyrics are practical but not precious. Li Houzhu has both beauties, and is even more enchanting with misty waters.

The Song people compared Fang Weng to Taibai, but he said "not even three or four out of ten." Regarding Su and Xin, he said, "Although the lyrics are called Su and Xin together, Xin is actually better than Su. Su's poetry is hurt by learning, and his lyrics are hurt by talent." Regarding Yang Tieya's Yuefu, he said, "It is another kind of peculiar writing. It is not appropriate to call it Yuefu, and so is Li Bin." Commenting on Zhao Wenmin's poetry, he said, "Not only is he a leader among the Yuan people, but he can be compared to Yan Tongshu in the Song Dynasty." And regarding Yu Zishan and Ouyang Xiu, he further compared them and said:

Yu Zishan's sentences are all based on allusions and are not flexible, while Ouyang Xiu forbids the use of even one allusion, so he becomes bland and empty, with no meaning at all.

In these places, you can see Nalan Chengde's brilliant views on poetry. Regarding Right Poetry and Yuefu, he also discussed them a lot, such as saying "Han people's Yuefu are mostly rich and treacherous, the Nineteen Old Poems are all noble and淡, " and "Jiaozhongqing's wife is also a different style in Yuefu." In particular, his opinions on Shaoling's Yuefu:

Shaoling's self-created new Yuefu is indeed a outstanding person of all time.

This judgment and his views on poetry are most easily seen to be consistent. Nalan Chengde criticized ancient lyricists, emphasizing the place where he expressed his originality, and his arguments were mostly so strong.

Five

Nalan Chengde also had many opinions on the overall criticism of poetry in various dynasties. For example, he commented on Song lyrics: "Since the wars of the Five Dynasties, the Central Plains drama has withered, the way of poetry has been lost, and the short lyrics have flourished greatly. The Song people specialized in lyrics, which were truly exquisite. Their poetry was like dust-covered rice and mud-smeared soup, so it was far inferior to the Tang people." This judgment cannot be said to have no problems, because the rise of Song lyrics was definitely not due to just these two reasons, but in many places, it was also a "unique insight," as another article says:

The Elegies and Odes mostly use allegory, and the Songs of the States mostly use comparison and metaphor: the Songs of Chu came out of the Songs of the States, purely using comparison and metaphor, with very little allegory; Tang poetry followed the style of Elegies and Odes, mostly using comparison and metaphor; Song poetry used less comparison and metaphor; Ming poetry is all allegory, and it feels stale and tasteless.

Nalan Chengde's discussion of Yuefu is also quite interesting. Many articles involve this issue, with opinions, explanations, and doubts. He pointed out that Yuefu was the name established by Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty, not the poetry and rites that later people considered to be poetry and rites. He also said that, in general, ancient poems were specially written for music and singing, called Yuefu; there were also literary men who occasionally wrote, and the musicians composed music and sang them, which were also called Yuefu. He also said that many people today cannot understand the topic of Yuefu, so there is no need to force them to do it; Li Yulin's imitation of Youmeng's clothing only made people laugh. These opinions may be based on some evidence and can allow us to see his diligent research attitude. At the same time, in Lushuiting Miscellaneous Records, it is explained that not only Yuefu can be sung, but poetry, lyrics, and songs have all had extremely holy times of singing.

Song people's lyrics, but the Tang people's method of singing poetry was abandoned; when Yuan Qu arose, they were both abandoned, and when Southern Qu arose, Northern Qu was also abandoned: the songs of today are like the Ming Deer and dust-covered rice.

Historical poetry was also discussed in Lushuiting Miscellaneous Records, and some very research-oriented opinions were provided. In Nalan Chengde's opinion, the intention is to be intentional without falling into discussion. Once there is discussion, it becomes historical criticism. He also said that the events in one's own story should only be used in the poems about history, and the events in another's story must be clearly distinguished between the host and the guest. If they are only used as ancient events, it is not appropriate to do so. The text must show the meaning, and the meaning must be in the text, without revealing the intention.

The Two Brothers (6)(5)

— Guy de Maupassant, translated by Li Weike

Jean immediately stood up:

"I'm not crazy, but I've had enough of your face."

Pierre mocked him:

"You've had enough? Are you part of Mrs. Lehau?"

"You need to know that Mrs. Lehau is about to become my wife."

The other laughed even harder!

"Ah! Ah! Great. I now know why I shouldn't call her "widow" anymore. But you used a strange way to inform me of your marriage."

"I won't allow you to joke... Do you hear me... I won't allow you to joke?"

Jean walked closer, pale, his voice trembling. He was even more enraged by the continued mockery of the woman he loved, the woman he had chosen.

But Pierre suddenly became equally furious. All the pent-up anger, suppressed resentment, recently restrained revulsion, and silent grief in his heart surged into his mind, making him seem congested and deranged.

"You dare?…… You dare?…… I order you to shut your beak, do you hear me, I order you to shut your beak!"

Jean, not expecting him to be so violent, was silent for a moment, searching in the confused thoughts that we have when we are in great anger for words and phrases that could directly wound his brother's heart.

He tried to calm himself down so that he could strike with more force, trying to speak slowly so that his words would sound more sharp:

"I've known for a long time that you're jealous of me. I've known it since the day you started calling her "widow," because you knew that title was hurting me."

Pierre let out the sharp, contemptuous laugh he was used to:

"Ah! Ah! God! I'm jealous of you!…… Me?…… Me?…… Me?…… What am I jealous of you for?…… What am I jealous of you for?…… God! Am I jealous of your face or your brain?……"

But Jean knew he had touched his sore spot:

"That's right, you're jealous of me. You've been jealous of me since you were a child: you got angry when you saw this woman choose me and not you."

Pierre was so enraged by this speculation that he couldn't speak clearly:

"I…… I…… I'm jealous of you? For this stupid thing, for this bastard woman, for this fat goose?……"

Jean, seeing that his words had hit him, continued:

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Admonition Against Smoking

— Wu

I haven't written talks for a long time, and I always feel itchy. On the one hand, it is because now is the year to only talk about wind and moon. People who write articles must have a skill in praising and admiring, such as favorable weather and national peace. But I am ashamed to say that this is really beyond my expertise, and there is no way, so I have to put down my pen. But on the other hand, it is indeed too lazy (I dare not say busy). Therefore, I simply think that everything is going well. In fact, it is ultimately because there is nothing to talk about. Fortunately, this time I spent a morning's effort to think of such a safe and sound topic.

Admonishing against smoking is exactly the same as admonishing against whoring and gambling. It is not like accumulating Yin merits, so I feel more at ease.

Recently, I have indeed been like this. Whenever I see a friend smoking, I sincerely and earnestly advise him: "Friend, quit smoking, why bother?" But every time it is the same, the friend immediately replies to me: "You advise me to quit smoking? Why don't you advise yourself?" Really, it is quite funny to think about it. Isn't it true that everyone would laugh out tears if a procuress taught a prostitute to be a respectable woman? But I still advise people to quit smoking and write articles against smoking. I would not dare to be so bold without a full reason.

To put it a little further, I do not know that advising people to quit smoking is a very sinful thing. For example, take myself. If I don't have money to buy vegetables, I can eat tofu without soy sauce, but I can't not smoke. Especially when my right hand is holding a pen and writing something on paper, my left hand must have a Golden Mouse brand cigarette, otherwise I cannot fill a five-hundred-word manuscript paper. From this, it can be seen that tobacco is truly too destined for those who play with pen and ink.

Furthermore, I must smoke when playing five hundred, I must smoke when sitting in the Great World listening to Yuan Yuan's singing, I must smoke when talking about worldly affairs with old friends, I must smoke when attending a tea party, and I must smoke when going to the toilet to shit, and I must smoke even more when reading "Tears and Laughter Marriage" or "Outside the Circle of Love"... In this way, the benefits of smoking are great! How can one quit?

But recently, after listening to a friend surnamed He say, "Let's quit smoking," this reminded me that in China, tobacco really can't be smoked anymore. At that time, it was like this: I said, "Why quit smoking?" He said well, "Don't you know? Because of the bandit suppression donation? Cigarettes have gone up in price again." That night, after waking up in the middle of the night, urinating once, and going back to bed, I secretly smoked a cigarette and couldn't help but think about the day's events, so I carefully calculated it. The current Golden Mouse brand is fifteen copper coins a box, with ten cigarettes, which is exactly fifteen big coins per cigarette. If you buy it retail, it is three copper coins for two cigarettes, so you don't need to find change. But when the price goes up, it will at least become seventeen cash per cigarette. Fifty cash for three cigarettes, the cigarette store will definitely not do it, one hundred and twenty cash for seven cigarettes, there is no reason for that either. After calculating, it is either four copper coins for two cigarettes, or twenty cash per cigarette. If this goes on, the cigarette store will of course be smiling because they can earn a few more dollars, but the smokers will inevitably be out of luck. At least they will have to smoke two fewer cigarettes from their daily habit of ten cigarettes so that they will not exceed their monthly budget.

Going a step further, it is better to quit smoking, because donating money to kill people is ultimately a matter of damaging Yin virtues! If you can't quit, then you will have to switch to foreign cigarettes. Why? The reason is very clear.

As an attached statement, this article does not advise people to quit opium red pills. This is of course because they do not need to be advised. Those who have money to smoke opium donate silver dollars to buy poison gas cannons.

On Life

— Mu

The question of life occasionally floats into my mind, and I think about the past, the present, and the future... Various phenomena and problems stir up huge waves in my mind like the spring tide.

The past life 丨 the golden age of childhood was infinitely sweet, the more one remembers it, the better it seems, but the more one thinks about it, the more frustrated and sad one becomes, for the golden age of childhood can never be regained! The youthful days of adolescence were also infinitely sweet, studying, exercising, sightseeing, and even falling in love at school, enjoying the most carefree, wonderful, and happy happiness of life, 丨 which is also pleasing to remember, the more one thinks about it, the better, but the more one thinks about it, the more frustrated and sad one becomes, for the youthful days of adolescence can never be regained!

Leaving school life and stepping into society, one has tasted all the bitter, sour, and spicy flavors, 丨 although one has sometimes tasted sweet and wonderful flavors, 丨 which only makes you struggle for life all day long, fighting with society, and remembering it brings no benefit, only sadness, resentment, and depression!

As for the present life, the social environment oppresses you to the point of suffocation. If you are ignorant or careless enough to speak out your thoughts, then arrows and poisonous gas, rumors and slanders, open and secret attacks will launch a total assault, making it impossible for you to eat and live in peace! How can one have the freedom and happiness of birds in the sky and fish in the water!

If the present life is like this, will the future life be better? Just thinking about it is disheartening! Why do people have to be so exclusive, jealous, hateful, and attacking? If everyone pursues their own ideals and goes their own way, and if that's not possible, couldn't we at least love and help each other? Why doesn't everyone move towards this path of mutual love and help? As long as you think with a broad mind and long-term vision, whose ideals will be different? People suffer from shortsightedness, only looking at the present and not seeking the future. As a result, conflicts arise for the sake of immediate life, leading to exclusion, jealousy, hatred, and attacks between people. Therefore, the path of life is bitter! Therefore, everyone feels oppressed by the present life, and everyone feels vague about the future life. Everyone feels this way, which is actually caused by the thoughts and actions of each individual. Don't blame others, you yourself have created your life like this!

Let's overthrow shortsightedness and broaden our horizons, let's shout.

Then, if everyone's ideals are the same, everyone loves and helps each other, and everyone's life is happy, all the demons and monsters in society will flee in panic, and society will be such a beautiful and bright place!

For the sake of life, everyone should walk towards this bright road!
