The Fur Coat

— Shi Ben

In this snobbish era of "only respecting clothes, not people," the issue of "clothing" is so important! Especially when working in government offices, people always say "impressive appearance," and the issue of "clothing" is even more important! As long as you are dressed a little shabbily, people will surely look down on you! Colleagues will try to push you down. Conversely, if you dress nicely, you will be respected, and colleagues will be friendly to you everywhere. This is a common and terrible phenomenon in today's snobbish society, and everyone knows it.

I work for a newspaper, and the four or five colleagues inside are all like bitter gourds bumping into each other. We are all struggling writers, and everyone is equally poor and embarrassed. Therefore, no one looks down on anyone. We don't care much about the quality of our clothes. However, because of the nature of my job, I have to interact with the outside world every day, so clothing becomes an issue. Because I was poorly dressed a few times, I always ended up with people "disdaining to speak" when I went to interview for news! They would speak evasively and dishonestly, how could I get accurate news? I was extremely angry, but when I thought about it, "clothing" was indeed an important trick for interviewing news! I couldn't help but pay attention to it. So, I started to care about my clothes, and most of my salary was spent on "clothing." It's hard! In the past two years, I have been exhausted trying to maintain this poor facade, and I owe a lot of money. I worry about it day and night. Alas! "Dressed in silk, but no rice for dinner at home," I, who used to be frugal, am now just like my old friends on Zhengjia Muqiao in Shanghai.

In the past two days, the west wind has started to blow, and the weather has suddenly turned cold. Everything in the world has changed. People are even busier with their preparations. Rich people with money have fur coats, cotton clothes, fireplaces, and radiators, which have emerged in response to the season. Poor me, trying to maintain a facade, is still wearing a camel hair robe. Walking on the road in the early morning and late at night, the cold wind is bone-chilling, and the cold dew cracks my skin. I deeply feel the cruel coercion of nature. Every time the northwest wind blows, I think that the weather is so cold, the camel hair robe is already outdated. If I wear it when I go to see people, won't they look down on me again? But, if I take off this camel hair robe, what can I replace it with? Wasn't the black sheepskin robe I wore last year pawned at "Yi Liu Bank" in the spring because the landlady was urging me to pay the rent? I plan to redeem it and wear it now, but where can I get the principal of twenty dollars at once? As for the monthly salary of twenty dollars from the newspaper, it is used to cover the living expenses of my wife and me, oil, salt, firewood, rice, rent, and social expenses. In this era of high living costs, what is it enough for? Therefore, since last year, I have been pawning and borrowing money, living a "borrowing from tomorrow to pay for today" life every day. So, even if I have twenty dollars in salary next month, I won't have any extra money to redeem this fur coat. But, if I don't redeem it, it won't do. First, the weather is getting colder, and a camel hair robe is not enough to keep warm after all. Second, appearance is important. It's too embarrassing not to wear a fur coat in the cold weather. Moreover, didn't my colleagues Jianqiu and Tianmei advise me yesterday: "You should try to redeem this fur coat, because when a person works in society, this facade must be maintained! If you really don't wear a fur coat this year, people will say behind your back: 'So-and-so is in trouble this year, he hasn't even put on a fur coat.' Then people will look down on you, and your reputation will be greatly affected." I knew all along that in this society of "only respecting clothes, not people," a fur coat is indeed very important. Whether you wear it or not affects your reputation! But, I can't maintain this poor facade this year. I have been planning for more than twenty dollars for many days, but I still haven't found a solution. I have nothing left to pawn, and I have no place to borrow money. I have exhausted all my resources, what else can I do? In the past two days, I have been so worried about this fur coat problem that I can't eat or sleep, I am sad and heartbroken, and I can't think of any solution. Alas! The oppression of material things is so profound!

Talking About Roads

— Yi

The first unpleasant thing when walking from the concession to the Chinese-controlled area under our government is that the roads are different. The roads in the concession are only wet after it rains, while the roads in the Chinese-controlled area are muddy and impassable after it rains. Could it be that roads also have a distinction between domestic and imported products? This year, the business community in Shanghai, especially the silk industry, has been shouting at the top of their lungs to promote "Domestic Goods Year." At the same time, the Ministry of Finance of the National Government is issuing lottery tickets to raise funds for the construction of aviation highways. I wonder if the money raised will actually be used to build highways in the future (I won't talk about aviation here). Will they still build some domestic roads? Although I am ignorant, I would like to offer a suggestion, as even a fool's thoughts may have some merit. Since it is said to be highway construction, the roads in the Chinese-controlled area are naturally different, but don't even mention highways. Whenever highways are mentioned, the roads are always rugged and uneven. When the weather is sunny, dust flies, and when it rains, mud splashes. Which highway is not equally corrupt? If the money raised from the lottery tickets is actually used to build highways, I think at least a model highway should be built across the country, with a solid foundation and the surface covered with asphalt. Then, travel will be convenient, and driving public buses will not make people worry about being injured in the buttocks and internal organs. By all means, do not build domestic roads.

Speaking of highways and public buses, it reminds me of the relationship between cars and roads. There is something called a Road Association, I don't know if it is a private organization or a publicly funded one. When they hold exhibitions, in addition to promoting roads, they also specifically promote foreign cars. I used to suspect that it was subsidized by the American Ford Motor King, but now I know that there is not much relationship. Even if it is related to foreign car companies, it is not surprising. Once roads are built, they are bound to be used for vehicles. The domestic single-wheeled wooden carts and two-wheeled horse-drawn carriages have been eliminated, and the need for cars is undoubtedly supported. Since Chinese people have not yet established factories to manufacture cars, it is clear and obvious that imported cars should be adopted. In this way, promoting road construction should logically and rightfully promote foreign cars, who would dare to criticize it. Moreover, although domestic cars have not yet been manufactured in factories, there are already public buses assembled with foreign parts. However, how unreliable and durable are those domestic products, how can they catch up with the quality of foreign cars? China must purchase foreign cars to build roads. This is the knowledge of experts, so they dare not monopolize it and offer it to the Chinese people and promote it. How sufficient, thorough, profound, and righteous is the reasoning? However, let's not talk about it. It is beneficial to others and harmless to oneself, which is the essence of morality in your country, and I also support it. The so-called people who benefit are the international imperialists, which is also in line with the spirit of international technical cooperation of our National Government, and should be greatly supported. However, why don't the capitalists of our Chinese industrial sector jointly set up factories to manufacture cars to compete with foreign cars in the market and recover our rights and interests? Some people say that the capital of our Chinese national bourgeoisie has already been controlled and oppressed by the financial power of international imperialism. They are in this semi-colonial country and have no chance to turn over and raise their heads, so the industry and commerce are depressed. This statement may be true. Then, since the government wants to build highways, why not even manufacture the cars that run on the highways? If the government sets up factories to manufacture cars, and at the same time raises tariffs on imported foreign cars, the car business is also a great source of profit. Then, the lottery tickets issued by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government to raise funds for the construction of aviation highways should be changed to the name of constructing highways and manufacturing cars, and the large sum of money should be used for constructing highways and manufacturing cars. I think this humble suggestion of mine will surely be supported by most of my compatriots. The reason is that constructing aviation has no real benefit for our common people. If we buy airplanes and do not go to deal with the imperialist enemies but start a civil war and drop bombs on our common people, this is even more unacceptable.

My Future Plans

— Yizhi

Although this year is the Year of Domestic Goods, it can also be said to be the Year of Plans. Look, one plan here, another plan there, plans are springing up like bamboo shoots after a rain, becoming more and more numerous every day. But what are they planning? This is determined by each person's position. Generally, what the party and state dignitaries are planning, in addition to building villas and marrying wives, is nothing more than pacifying the country internally and resisting foreign aggression externally, benefiting the country and the people. The Guangzhou ×× Three-Year Plan and the Central ×× Whole Plan are plans for pacifying the country internally and resisting foreign aggression externally, benefiting the country and the people. What the military men are planning, in addition to plundering, is nothing more than expanding their territory and extending their influence. What the capitalists are planning is nothing more than selling counterfeit goods as domestic goods and deceiving customers with big discounts. What the bourgeois class is planning is nothing more than leisure and enjoyment. Only those poor and suffering friends still have no plans. Perhaps they have no reason to plan even if they want to. In short, planning is as popular and modern today as a modern girl wearing a fur-collared coat.

I am not a party and state dignitary, nor am I a person who specializes in plundering and enjoying pleasure. Originally, I am not qualified to have plans. However, I think that planning is not limited to the present, and everything in the future can be planned in advance. Therefore, I have a preliminary plan for the future:

(1) Write more articles praising local officials, so that I can be favored by them and give up my writing career to join the army.

(2) Do not discuss national politics, do not talk about military affairs, only write flattering articles, only write poems about love and romance, so that there will be no danger.

(3) Stay at home all year round, not taking a step beyond the bounds, because during this period of pacifying the country, stepping out of the house means risking being hit by stray bullets from the police catching thieves on the road, so if I want to go out, I must wear an iron helmet and a suit of armor to prevent accidents.

(4) Tell my beautiful and graceful sister to go to dance halls more often and go to the movies more often. Once she gains the love of a big man, I can rely on her connections to get lucky.

(5) I run a domestic goods store, but I can't help but stock up on Eastern, European, and American goods to pass off fake goods as genuine. This is the only way for merchants to make a fortune.

(6) Spend a lot of money to marry a star as a concubine, so that I can improve my reputation and make people envy my good fortune in love.

If I proceed according to the above plan, ten years later, if I am not a popular person in society, I must be an idiot.

Novel

Shanghai (2) (4)

— Zhang Lao San

(36) Trouble Maker

A tram came and cut off the conversation. There were only two passengers in the first-class carriage besides the ticket seller. I occupied a corner of the carriage, and Sister Hui sat next to me. When buying tickets, she touched her pocket, smiled, and said to me, "I didn't bring any money." I glanced at her, paid for two military tickets, and didn't say anything.

"I didn't plan to come out," Cousin continued.

"Such hospitality is too sincere."

Cousin lowered her head. Temporarily silent, the car quickly moved forward.

A white man came in at the Foch Road station. The exotic atmosphere of Zhenfei Road was already visible in front of us. As the car approached the second stop, Cousin rummaged through her pocket and took out a letter to give to me. She looked flustered and said, "This is the letter you wrote to me." She blushed and looked out the window, being stared at by the tall nose opposite. The car stopped at the second stop, and a group of passengers poured in. The carriage suddenly became lively. I didn't have a chance to read the returned letter, so I stuffed it into my pocket and got off at Luban Road.

Today is Sunday, and many friends came to the club. When we stepped in, my younger brother was holding Xiao Huang's arm. The crowd shouted in a mess, "Long live love!" Sister Hui ran to Sister Jing with bounding strides and grabbed her hand, asking her what was so funny. I, who was walking slowly into the living room behind, was completely baffled by this sudden change of attitude.

Xiao Huang pulled down the hand of my younger brother hanging on her arm and ran upstairs as if she was worried about something. Before I could pay attention to him, Gao Fei shouted:

"The trouble maker ran away again!"

Xiao Feng and Chongqing remembered the trouble of the love triangle, looked at Sister Min and Sister Hui standing opposite each other, and then shifted their gazes to me, as if telling me what was being teased here. I, who was in a very suspicious position at this time, didn't dare to say an ordinary word, because an unnecessary misunderstanding might be caused by an ordinary word. When I walked to the table and took out a cigarette, Sister Min and Sister Hui, who were acting antagonistically, greeted everyone and jumped upstairs, seemingly sticking to their positions.

The room was suddenly silent. Gao Fei pulled me to sit on the sofa and told me that after I left in the morning, Sister Min looked for you everywhere and didn't even eat lunch, but she wasn't angry on the surface. Our friends were teasing her about the love triangle. Did you really go to Huiqin's place?

I nodded, not knowing whether I was expressing "yes" or "I know." I stood up and paced back and forth in the living room. The cigarette butt burned my fingers before I threw it into the spittoon.

The second cigarette was in my hand, and I was still pacing back and forth in the room. The tea room attendant, Afu, came down from upstairs and asked me, "Mr. Li, would you like to have egg fried rice?"

"Dinner has been served," I looked at Gao Fei and said.

"It's almost two o'clock, Mr. Li. Miss Xu said you haven't eaten either."

"Okay," I raised my head and looked at the clock on the wall, it was five minutes to two.

Movie Special

A Glimpse into Mae West's Private Life

— Jia Ke

Her appearance reveals supreme romance

But her heart is extremely upright

Mae West's "I'm No Angel" has finished its run at the Cathay Theatre, and is now playing for several days at the Carlton. It seems that after sweeping through America, it has come to sweep through China, making many Shanghai movie fans intoxicated in her bewitching and dissolute performance for two hours. What is the impression that people get after seeing Mae West's movies? What do they guess about her personal private life? I am afraid that everyone always thinks that she must be an extremely romantic and unrestrained woman, right? This is not to blame everyone. Originally, various American film magazines have a lot of publicity about Mae West's personal life, deliberately making it cloudy and rainy, making it unpredictable. In fact, those are the promotional techniques of film merchants. It is said that Mae West herself is indeed a well-behaved woman. There are three film actors who have co-starred with Mae West, and kissed her on the screen. They are now coming out to prove it.

Before going to Hollywood, Mae West was originally a star on the Broadway stage. One of those who have performed with her on stage is Arthur Vinton. He co-starred with Mae West in many famous plays, and I won't list them all here. He said, "When I was assigned to contact Mae West for co-starring, I was initially very reluctant, because I felt that she was a very difficult woman to approach. But for the sake of my work, I finally went to see her. Unexpectedly, after talking to her, I found that she was indeed a down-to-earth woman. On the surface of her most feminine body, she has the most masculine brain. This is where she is great. The agility of her mind is like the trigger on a pistol. No matter what you say or what you are planning, she always chases ahead of you. As for the various rumors outside, they are not true. Her few characteristics are: being punctual, not being afraid of hard work, treating people with humility and politeness, and never being arrogant. And in general, colleagues are very polite to her, because she is not someone who can be messed with casually. No matter what the time, people always call her Miss West, and no one calls her just Mae. And when she calls people, she always adds the title of Mr. As for saying that she is a seductive woman, I can say that anyone who has been close to her can know that it is not true."

Generally, a woman who is naturally lewd must have a very vicious heart, but Mae West's heart is infinitely kind. She often does not hesitate to spend her own money and energy to help people. She can be considerate of people, help people, and never have selfish intentions. The following is the word of Jack la Rue. He co-starred with Mae West in (Diamond Lil). He talks about how he was able to be Mae West's supporting role. At that time, Mae West was looking for a Spanish boy. He was Italian, but a good actor. His contract was about to expire, and he was anxiously looking for something to do. Being Mae West's supporting role was the best hope. So he went to see Mae West. Mae asked him if he was Spanish. He answered with a few Spanish words that he learned from a speed learning association. She also asked him if he could perform. He said he was willing to try his skills on the spot. So they performed on the spot. After the performance, Mae West said: Not bad, not bad. She asked him when he could start auditioning. Jack said he had a long-term contract with a company. Mae West was very surprised. If he had a long-term contract with another company, why did he come to see her? Jack said that if the money was more, he would rather give up the long-term contract and cooperate with her. Mae West agreed to everything, and Jack's salary was very high, beyond his own expectations. However, after they auditioned several times, she investigated everything clearly. She knew that he was not Spanish, and that he did not have any long-term contract. Obviously, she was deceived. But she didn't hate him. Instead, she saw him and laughed. She said that when a person has no way to go, it is forgivable to play a trick occasionally. Therefore, Jack was very grateful to her.

There is also Russell Hardil, who has co-starred with Mae West in countless plays on the screen or on the stage. He also proves that Mae West is a very upright person. He has never seen her behave in a lewd manner outside of the stage or screen. She likes to joke and have fun, that is true, but she has never lost the respect of others. Her use of "sex" to perform is something that others cannot achieve, and is something that others dare not do. Apart from Mae West, if others want to learn from her, not only will they absolutely not be able to learn, but there are also many dangers. The fact that she did not fall into the miscellaneous troupe, or a more humble position, but was able to achieve her current lofty position is what makes her great and unattainable.

Film Review

Review of "Evil Neighbor"

— Ling He

| Moonlight Production, Carlton Premiere |

(1)

First, I must discuss with Mr. Fasi, the playwright of "Evil Neighbor." Is it truly because China has embraced Western material civilization and abandoned the old morality of national essence that it has become so fragmented, leading to its imminent demise? I believe this is the author's biggest conceptual mistake.

We can say with certainty that so-called old morality and spiritual civilization are the superstructure built upon the economic foundation. Now, the economic system has developed from rural economy to capitalism. Then, the old morality of the superstructure must necessarily change its essence with the transformation of the economic system. That is to say, old morality will never continue to be effective under the existing economic system. This is the same reason why feudal emperors cannot survive in capitalist society. Old morality has naturally disappeared completely, and material civilization is also inevitably the most rational product of the current society. Obviously, the old is only destroyed, and the new is growing rapidly. This is an ironclad historical decision that no one can ignore.

So, why is there an exception in China? Could it be said that the rural economy in China has not suffered destruction?

(2)

Therefore, China's poverty and weakness, China's being divided and slaughtered, are definitely not because of the decline of old morality or because it should not have accepted Western material civilization. The only reason is that China's current status is that of a semi-feudal and semi-colonial state.

Indeed, "Evil Neighbor" expresses opposition to the aggression of strong neighbors, but taking narrow nationalism as a premise is already a dead end, not to mention the author's erroneous understanding as mentioned above?

(3)

Due to the seriousness of the errors mentioned above, I cannot help but point them out more strictly. I think this is the critic's most important responsibility in guiding the audience. In fact, audiences with low levels of knowledge will go down the wrong path because of its distortion.

In addition, I strongly disagree with the author's purely symbolic approach to dealing with this issue. For example, representing Japan as the evil neighbor, the township council as the League of Nations, "Zhong Guofen" as the Chinese soul, "Huang Huaren" as the Yellow race, "Bai Jinji" as the economy of the white race, "Wu Zhihua" as matter, and "Cai Mafu" as certain national heroes. Because of this, it completely loses its seriousness and activeness. Of course, everything is not free at the moment, but positive depictions should still be made within the possible range.

(4)

In terms of filmmaking techniques, Moonlight Company has indeed made some progress compared to the past, whether in photography, performance, or set design. However, they are still obsessed with martial arts fights (allegedly for sales in Nanyang and the mainland). This cannot be praised in terms of martial arts techniques, and in this respect, what difference is there from the recently premiered "Six Episodes of Female Escort"? I believe that not abandoning martial arts fights is always a loss for Moonlight Company.

As for individual actors, the one who played Huang Huaren is the best, followed by Wang Feijuan, who is also natural.

(5)

In addition, I think that the "Shaw's humor, Hitler's tragedy" etc. on the instructions are not a clever publicity method. Also, most of the so-called "humorous subtitles" are not visible in the film.

Furthermore, it should be added that in yesterday's first show, there were two Japanese people there watching very enthusiastically, and I heard them talking very indignantly. From this, it can be seen that the Japanese are very attentive to movies, truly so-called caring people are meticulous.

Review of "History of the Great War in Europe"

— Moore

Hells "Holiday"

Friche said in "Twentieth Century European Literature": "One of the main components of the ideological structure of imperialist literature is the praise of violence and war." This is not necessarily a clear example in literature, but it is also reflected in movies. Their essential means is to beautify war, emphasize the national concept of the masses, and erase the tragic scenes of war.

However, amid the rumbling of cannons, those who die in batches are only the hardworking people. Beautiful deception can no longer withstand the attack of facts. Thus, outstanding writers "dropped the hammer of truth on the hypocrisy, cruelty, and blood caused by war." (Gorky) Henry Barbusse's novel "Under Fire" depicts the transformation of international war to revolutionary war. And after painful reflection, Remarque and others also wrote his humanitarian "All Quiet on the Western Front," and it was quickly made into a movie.

The great war of 1936, predicted by international politicians, will begin in the Far East. At this time, every character is "itching to fight" and "preparing to fight." So, they quickly reviewed the old lessons of the European war. On the one hand, the newsreels of that time had lost their timeliness, so they were edited and added to become new films to make money. There have been many such films recently. "The Blood Battle History of Xing Dengbao" is famous, and currently we are seeing this "History of the Great War in Europe."

As the advertisement claims, this film was actually shot on location. Because it was originally a newsreel, it was only an objective existence. After being produced once, it has been injected with subjectivity. In other words, the writer has already expressed his opinion on this existence. Now, in "History of the Great War in Europe," we only see the power of cannons, but not the suffering of the people. Even if we see smoke rising, it seems to only form the conditions for this "power" and this "spectacle." From this, we can see the producer's intention is to "review old lessons," not to feel sorrow for the old events. This can naturally be said to be due to the newsreels of that time, but precisely because it is a newsreel of that time, it is a praise of war, and our writers use it, which more accurately explains the meaning.

Recently, "anti-war films" have been opposed by some. Naturally, only war can eliminate war, but we must pay attention that only revolutionary national wars are what we should expand, while imperialist mutual robbery wars and intervention wars are what we should oppose. If there is a promotion of "killing" and "drinking blood" for other purposes, it will only plunge the people into a bottomless abyss, and the result is to consolidate the position of the privileged (imperialists and others). The outbreak of the Second World War is just around the corner. From the "History of the Great War in Europe," we see their conspiracy! Audiences! "Not in war, until the war, must form brothers!" (Barbusse) We are against imperialist war!

Listen, Husbands of the World

— Xi Fu

In Wall Street, New York, USA, there is a rich man named Stephen Ames. Because he is generous and blessed, Hollywood considers him "one of the million husbands." What is the reason? It's very interesting to talk about. Stephen has a beautiful wife, and she wanted to go to Hollywood to make movies two years ago. Stephen, because she begged him so many times, couldn't bear to go against her wishes, so he agreed generously. That wife is the famous Adrienne Ames. But a female star, if she lacks a male companion, is extremely inconvenient in social situations. But he himself holds an important position in the financial world of New York, making a lot of money every day, how can he give up his position to accompany his star wife? So, he listened to his wife again and agreed to hire a rising star, Bruce Cabot, as his wife's official male companion, so that he could enter and exit social occasions. Later, Bruce and Adrienne gradually turned friendship into love and became inseparable. So Stephen specially ran to Hollywood for this matter, acting as a matchmaker for them, and he retreated to the ranks of friends. It is said that Bruce and Adrienne, after Stephen's persuasion, will get married soon. Isn't this spirit of selflessness admirable?

Movie Novel

24 Hours in Shanghai (1)

— Tian Fu

Directed by Shen Xiling, produced by Star Film Company

Starring Zhu Qiuhen, Zhou Boxun, Chen Ningqiu, Zhao Dan, Gu Meijun, and Gu Lanjun

(1) A Small Matter

4 p.m., when the arteries of the metropolis beat most violently. Cars are connected to trams, and trams are connected to cars: Looking down from the top of a skyscraper: they are two straight lines of ants crawling towards each other...

At this time, a foreign-funded yarn factory is busy. The current of the motor is flowing, and the large axles pull the belts to circulate endlessly. Under the spinning wheels sit a row of female workers, each one's hands are mechanically moving, tense faces, smiling faces, and faces with melancholic anemia. Children picking up yarn under the belt pulleys. It is said that childhood is the "golden age" of life, and the "golden age" of these child laborers is spent in the work of picking up yarn.

Suddenly丨A piece of clothing was brought out on the rapidly rotating belt, and thrown violently into the air. Then there was a sharp scream, which was emitted in the heavy sound of the machine wheel.

At this time, the workers in the entire factory stopped like a machine braking and immediately rushed forward to surround the injured and fallen child. The child's face was pale, and the floor was covered in blood.

"Number 39 is crushed!" "Number 39 is crushed!"

Everyone shouted in panic. A young female worker drilled into the crowd. She suddenly squatted down, hugged the injured lamb, and cried sadly: "Brother! Brother!"

The air in the factory became miserable. In this commotion, the supervisor calmly ran in with the doctor. The doctor looked at the child's injury.

"Is it okay?" A tearful female worker's face looked at the doctor anxiously. But the doctor did not speak, he shook his head gently.

(2) Comprador and Wife

This is a noble and beautiful gentleman, Mr. Zhou, the comprador of the yarn factory.

He is listening to the phone. The sound of the foreman speaking carefully came from the telephone receiver, reporting the matter of a child laborer being crushed in the workshop. This report caused a look of anger to flash across the comprador's face. He was not happy to hear these.

"Is there a need to report this? It's their own carelessness, what's there to say!" After answering like this, he put down the receiver. He leisurely flipped through the movie advertisements in the newspaper:

As if thinking of something happy, the comprador suddenly smiled. Then he made a phone call. This phone call was to the comprador's residence. The comprador's wife was lying lazily in bed, gently stroking the docile pug lying next to her with one hand, and picked up the phone on the table with the other.

The comprador's voice from the telephone: "There shouldn't be any prior engagements today, my wife, how about we go to the movies?"

The wife thought for a while, twisted her body, and said charmingly into the phone:

"Um, no, Mrs. Li invited me to her house to play cards today."... (To be continued)
